  title="Static table checklist for semantic flow"
  columns={["Table", "Required", "Purpose"]}
  rows={[
    ["ce_config", "Yes", "DefaultSemanticAstGenerator prompts/schema (SYSTEM_PROMPT, USER_PROMPT, SCHEMA_PROMPT)."],
    ["ce_intent", "Yes", "SEMANTIC_QUERY intent registration."],
    ["ce_intent_classifier", "Yes", "Route semantic questions to SEMANTIC_QUERY."],
    ["ce_prompt_template", "Yes", "SCHEMA_JSON and DERIVED templates for SEMANTIC_QUERY."],
    ["ce_response", "Yes", "COMPLETED/FAILED response mapping."],
    ["ce_rule", "Yes", "ANALYZE bootstrap + MCP outcome transitions + reset behavior."],
    ["ce_mcp_tool", "Yes", "Register db.semantic.query in MCP scope."],
    ["ce_mcp_planner", "Yes", "Planner prompt for SEMANTIC_QUERY/ANALYZE."],
    ["ce_verbose", "Yes", "Stage + AST LLM + runtime determinant messaging."],
    ["ce_output_schema", "Optional", "Extraction helper schema for semantic prompts."]
  ]}
/>

### Application YAML required

```yaml
mcp:
  db:
    query:
      mode: semantic # semantic-catalog | knowledge-graph | semantic

    semantic-catalog:
      enabled: true

    knowledge-graph:
      enabled: true

    semantic:
      enabled: true
      model-path: classpath:/mcp/semantic-layer.yaml
```

## Request flow by package (quick reference)

1. `runtime/handler`: `DbSemanticQueryToolHandler` receives `db.semantic.query`.
2. `runtime/core + runtime/pipeline + runtime/stage/*`: `SemanticQueryRuntimeService` runs stage DAG.
3. `retrieval/*`: ranks candidate entity/tables.
4. `graph/*`: resolves join edges/path.
5. `llm/*`: generates AST JSON.
6. `ast/*`: canonicalize + normalize + validate.
7. `sql/*`: deterministic compile + policy.
8. `execute/*`: SQL run + row map.
9. `summary/*`: final user-facing summary payload.
10. `model/*`: shared semantic-layer model registry.

## Semantic Query runtime path

<div className="ce-dbkg-runtime-path">

<Highlight type="info" title="Full runtime lifecycle">
This is the complete end-to-end Semantic Query path for one turn. It follows the same Database Knowledge Graph runtime style, but each stage is specific to semantic retrieval, AST generation, deterministic SQL compile, execution, and response shaping.
</Highlight>

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item">
    <span className="ce-step-badge-index">1</span>
    <span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>User request</span>
  </div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Ingress payload reaches ConvEngine with user text, conversation id, and input params.

**Session Mutations:** `userText`, `inputParams`, bootstrap context placeholders.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** `ce_conversation (R/W)`, `ce_audit (W)`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-1">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="ConversationController.message()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/api/controller/ConversationController.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`public ResponseEntity<ConversationResponse> message(@RequestBody ConversationRequest request) {
  return ResponseEntity.ok(conversationalEngine.process(request));
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultConversationalEngine.process()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/provider/DefaultConversationalEngine.java">
{`public ConversationResponse process(ConversationRequest request) {
  EngineSession session = sessionManager.loadOrCreate(request);
  enginePipelineFactory.getPipeline().execute(session);
  return session.toResponse();
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>HTTP payload is converted into an `EngineSession` with immutable conversation identity and mutable turn context.</li>
      <li>`userText`, optional `inputParams`, and request metadata are attached before any classifier or rule executes.</li>
      <li>Session bootstrap ensures downstream steps read and mutate a shared context map.</li>
      <li>Conversation state is loaded if conversation id exists; otherwise first-turn bootstrap is created.</li>
      <li>Audit context is opened so stage-level determinants are linked to this turn.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 1 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["HTTP body (R)", "Reads userText, conversationId, inputParams."], ["ce_conversation (R/W)", "Load existing conversation or bootstrap a new one."], ["ce_audit (W)", "Ingress lifecycle traces."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item">
    <span className="ce-step-badge-index">2</span>
    <span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>McpToolStep + McpPlanner</span>
  </div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Planner resolves semantic turn to `CALL_TOOL` with `tool_code=db.semantic.query`.

**Session Mutations:** `context.mcp.lifecycle.*`, `MCP_ACTION`, `MCP_TOOL_CODE`, planner observations.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** `ce_mcp_planner (R)`, `ce_mcp_tool (R)`, `ce_rule (R)`, `ce_audit (W)`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-2">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="McpToolStep.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/steps/McpToolStep.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`for (int i = 0; i < maxLoops; i++) {
  McpPlan plan = planner.plan(session, tools, observations);
  if (McpConstants.ACTION_ANSWER.equalsIgnoreCase(plan.action())) {
    writeFinalAnswerToContext(session, plan.answer());
    break;
  }
  CeMcpTool tool = registry.requireTool(plan.tool_code(), session.getIntent(), session.getState());
  String rowsJson = resolveExecutor(toolGroup).execute(tool, args, session);
  observations.add(new McpObservation(toolCode, rowsJson));
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="McpPlanner.plan()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/McpPlanner.java">
{`PromptTemplateContext ctx = PromptTemplateContext.builder()
  .templateName("McpPlanner")
  .mcpTools(toolsJson)
  .mcpObservations(obsJson)
  .build();
String planJson = llm.generateJsonStrict(...);
return normalizePlan(mapper.readValue(planJson, McpPlan.class));`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>`McpToolStep` runs PRE_AGENT_MCP rules so semantic flow can be state-gated.</li>
      <li>Enabled MCP tools are fetched for current intent and state.</li>
      <li>`McpPlanner` receives tool list + observations + context and emits strict JSON action.</li>
      <li>On `CALL_TOOL`, selected tool executes and observation is appended into MCP context.</li>
      <li>Loop continues until planner returns `ANSWER`, then `mcp.finalAnswer` is persisted.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 2 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["ce_mcp_planner (R)", "Planner prompt rows."], ["ce_mcp_tool (R)", "Tool registry + scope checks."], ["ce_rule (R)", "PRE/POST MCP transitions."], ["ce_audit (W)", "Planner and MCP lifecycle traces."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item">
    <span className="ce-step-badge-index">3</span>
    <span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>DbSemanticQueryToolHandler</span>
  </div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Bridge MCP DB tool invocation to semantic runtime.

**Session Mutations:** Question normalized from args/session.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** `convengine.mcp.db.semantic.*`, `ce_audit (W)`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-3">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DbSemanticQueryToolHandler.toolCode()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/handler/DbSemanticQueryToolHandler.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`public String toolCode() {
  ConvEngineMcpConfig.Db.Semantic cfg = ...;
  return cfg.getToolCode() == null || cfg.getToolCode().isBlank()
      ? "db.semantic.query" : cfg.getToolCode();
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DbSemanticQueryToolHandler.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/handler/DbSemanticQueryToolHandler.java">
{`public Object execute(CeMcpTool tool, Map<String, Object> args, EngineSession session) {
  String question = extractQuestion(args, session);
  return runtimeService.plan(question, session);
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>Handler is resolved by MCP DB executor by tool code.</li>
      <li>Question extraction order is deterministic: `question` -> `query` -> `user_input` -> `session.userText`.</li>
      <li>Handler intentionally avoids planner/retrieval/SQL logic; it is an adapter boundary.</li>
      <li>Delegates to `SemanticQueryRuntimeService.plan` with normalized question.</li>
      <li>This keeps runtime swappable without changing MCP core contracts.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 3 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["ce_audit (W)", "Tool-handler entry traces."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">4</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>SemanticQueryRuntimeService</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Orchestrate semantic stage pipeline and handle runtime errors.

**Session Mutations:** `retrieval`, `joinPath`, `ast`, `canonicalAst`, `compiledSql`, `execution`, `summary`, `_meta`, `_db`.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** mode and enable flags, `ce_audit (W)`, `ce_verbose (R)`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-4">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticQueryRuntimeService.plan()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/core/SemanticQueryRuntimeService.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`for (SemanticQueryStage stage : stagePipeline.stages()) {
  if (stage == null || !stage.supports(context)) continue;
  publishBefore(stageInterceptors, stage.stageCode(), session, context);
  try {
    stage.execute(context);
    publishAfter(stageInterceptors, stage.stageCode(), session, context);
  } catch (Exception stageError) {
    publishStageError(stage, context, session, stageError);
    throw stageError;
  }
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticStagePipelineFactory.init()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/pipeline/SemanticStagePipelineFactory.java">
{`List<SemanticQueryStage> ordered = dagOrderer.order(
  discoveredStages,
  SemanticQueryStage.class,
  "Semantic query stage pipeline",
  c -> false
);
this.pipeline = new SemanticStagePipeline(ordered);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>Runtime rejects call unless `mcp.db.query.mode=semantic` and semantic is enabled.</li>
      <li>Interceptors are sorted once and wrapped around each stage.</li>
      <li>DAG-ordered stages execute deterministically.</li>
      <li>Stage failures emit stage-specific error determinants with rich metadata.</li>
      <li>Final output contains stage artifacts for troubleshooting and UI trace rendering.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 4 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["ce_audit (W)", "Stage enter/exit/meta/error determinants."], ["ce_verbose (R)", "Determinant message lookup."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">5</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>SemanticRetrievalStage</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Retrieve semantic entity and candidate tables.

**Session Mutations:** `retrieval.candidateEntities`, `retrieval.candidateTables`, confidence.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** `semantic-layer.yaml`, optional embeddings/vector search, `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-5">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticRetrievalStage.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/stage/provider/SemanticRetrievalStage.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`SemanticEntityTableRetriever retriever = resolveRetriever(context);
RetrievalResult retrieval = retriever.retrieve(context.question(), context.session());
context.retrieval(retrieval);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSemanticEntityTableRetriever scoring" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/retrieval/provider/DefaultSemanticEntityTableRetriever.java">
{`double deterministic = rc.getSynonymWeight() * synonym
  + rc.getFieldWeight() * fields
  + rc.getIdPatternWeight() * idPattern
  + rc.getLexicalWeight() * lexical;
double total = rc.getDeterministicBlendWeight() * clamp01(deterministic)
  + rc.getVectorBlendWeight() * clamp01(vector);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <p>
      Retrieval is the stage that decides <strong>which semantic entity and tables</strong> the rest of the pipeline should trust.
      Everything downstream (join-path, AST quality, SQL compile quality) depends on this ranking.
    </p>

    <DbTable
      title="Retrieval behavior: without vector vs with vector"
      columns={["Mode", "What gets computed", "Strength", "Weakness"]}
      rows={[
        ["No vector (`mcp.db.semantic.vector.enabled=false`)", "Deterministic lexical scoring only: synonym overlap, field overlap, id-pattern boosts, description overlap.", "Very predictable and easy to debug.", "Can miss semantic paraphrases when words differ from YAML wording."],
        ["Vector enabled (`mcp.db.semantic.vector.enabled=true`)", "Deterministic lexical + embedding similarity from `ce_mcp_semantic_embedding` (`ENTITY` and `TABLE`).", "Better semantic recall for paraphrases and natural language variations.", "Needs embedding rows and model quality; slightly more moving parts."]
      ]}
    />

    <h4>Activation YAML</h4>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="Enable vector retrieval for semantic query" language="yaml" defaultOpen={true}>
{`mcp:
  db:
    query:
      mode: semantic
    semantic:
      enabled: true
      model-path: classpath:/mcp/semantic-layer.yaml
      vector:
        enabled: true
        feedback-enabled: true
        table: ce_mcp_semantic_embedding
        namespace-column: namespace
        target-type-column: target_type
        target-name-column: target_name
        embedding-column: embedding
        metadata-column: metadata_json
        max-results: 20`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>

    <h4>Behind-the-scenes workflow (no vector)</h4>
    <ol>
      <li>Resolve retriever bean via `@Order` + `supports(session)`.</li>
      <li>Tokenize question to normalized lowercase terms.</li>
      <li>For each semantic entity: compute deterministic score using synonyms + fields + lexical + id-pattern.</li>
      <li>For selected entities, score candidate tables using table-name + field-column lexical overlap.</li>
      <li>Apply thresholds + top-N limits and write `retrieval.candidateEntities` and `retrieval.candidateTables`.</li>
    </ol>

    <h4>Behind-the-scenes workflow (vector enabled)</h4>
    <ol>
      <li>Everything from no-vector mode still runs.</li>
      <li>Generate embedding for user question using `llmClient.generateEmbedding(question)`.</li>
      <li>Run pgvector lookup via `PostgresPgVectorSearchAdapter` for nearest `ENTITY` and `TABLE` rows.</li>
      <li>Blend deterministic score and vector score per candidate.</li>
      <li>If feedback vectors are enabled, apply additional `USER_QUERY` similarity boost (`feedbackVector`).</li>
      <li>Sort final blended scores and output final candidate lists.</li>
    </ol>

    <h4>How lexical matching works (with your semantic YAML)</h4>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="YAML features that lexical retrieval reads" language="yaml">
{`entities:
  DisconnectRequest:
    synonyms:
      - disconnect
      - disconnection
      - service termination
    fields:
      requestId:
        column: zp_request.zp_request_id
        description: unique request id
      downstreamStatus:
        column: zp_disconnect_order.downstream_status
        description: downstream orchestration status`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>

    <DbTable
      title="Lexical scoring signals"
      columns={["Signal", "Source in YAML/question", "Example"]}
      rows={[
        ["Synonym overlap", "question tokens vs `entities.*.synonyms`", "Question has `termination` -> matches `service termination` synonym."],
        ["Field overlap", "question tokens vs field keys + field descriptions + column names", "Question has `downstream status` -> matches `downstreamStatus` field."],
        ["Description lexical overlap", "question tokens vs entity description text", "Question has `failed disconnect` -> overlaps entity description words."],
        ["ID pattern boosts", "regex in question (`ZPR*`, `DON*`, `ZPDISC*`)", "`DON9001` boosts disconnect/order-related entity."]
      ]}
    />

    <h4>Score blending concept</h4>
    <p>Entity/table ranking uses weighted blending from config.</p>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="Retrieval score blend (conceptual)" language="java">
{`double deterministic = synonymWeight * synonym
  + fieldWeight * fields
  + idPatternWeight * idPattern
  + lexicalWeight * lexical;

double total = deterministicBlendWeight * clamp01(deterministic)
  + vectorBlendWeight * clamp01(vectorScore)
  + feedbackWeight * clamp01(feedbackVectorScore);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>

    <DbTable
      title="Where each score comes from"
      columns={["Score", "Produced by", "Used when"]}
      rows={[
        ["deterministic", "DefaultSemanticEntityTableRetriever lexical/id scoring", "Always"],
        ["vectorScore", "PostgresPgVectorSearchAdapter over `ce_mcp_semantic_embedding` (`ENTITY`,`TABLE`)", "When `vector.enabled=true` and embedding exists"],
        ["feedbackVectorScore", "Nearest `USER_QUERY` vectors from feedback memory", "When `vector.enabled=true` and `vector.feedback-enabled=true`"]
      ]}
    />

    <h4>Turn-by-turn mini example</h4>
    <DbTable
      title="Example: same question, without and with vector"
      columns={["Turn", "User input", "No-vector likely outcome", "Vector-enabled likely outcome"]}
      rows={[
        ["T1", "why termination failed for DON9001", "May rely on lexical `failed` + `DON9001`; if `termination` token is weak in YAML, ranking can be medium confidence.", "Vector similarity pulls `DisconnectRequest`/`zp_disconnect_order` higher because `termination` semantically matches disconnect domain."],
        ["T2", "show downstream status and team notes", "Lexical may still find correct fields, but ranking can vary if wording differs.", "Vector + lexical stabilizes candidate entity/tables and improves consistency of selected fields."],
        ["T3", "list failed requests from last 24h", "Good lexical hit, usually correct.", "Also correct; vector mainly helps robustness for alternate phrasing."]
      ]}
    />

    <p>
      Key point: Retrieval is a ranking stage. Vector does not replace lexical logic; it augments it to improve semantic recall.
      The output from this stage (`candidateEntities`, `candidateTables`, reasons, confidence) is the contract consumed by join-path and AST stages.
    </p>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 5 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["semantic-layer.yaml (R)", "Entity metadata, synonyms, fields."], ["pgvector (optional R)", "Vector similarity lookup."], ["ce_audit (W)", "RETRIEVAL_DONE determinant."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">6</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>SemanticJoinPathStage</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Resolve join path using schema graph traversal.

**Session Mutations:** `joinPath.baseTable`, `joinPath.edges`, `joinPath.requiredTables`, `joinPath.unresolvedTables`.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** graph adapter (`jgrapht`), DB FK metadata, `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-6">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultJoinPathResolver.doResolve()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/graph/provider/DefaultJoinPathResolver.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`String base = candidates.get(0).name();
for (String target : requiredTables) {
  if (base.equalsIgnoreCase(target)) continue;
  List<SchemaEdge> path = graph.shortestPath(base, target, maxHops);
  if (path == null || path.isEmpty()) unresolved.add(target);
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="JGraphTSchemaGraphEngine.shortestPath()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/graph/provider/JGraphTSchemaGraphEngine.java">
{`while (!queue.isEmpty()) {
  NodePath current = queue.poll();
  if (current.node().equals(toTable)) return toEdges(current.path());
  for (String next : neighbors(current.node())) {
    if (!visited.contains(next)) queue.add(new NodePath(next, nextPath));
  }
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>Base table is picked from top candidate table from retrieval stage.</li>
      <li>Required tables are resolved from selected candidates.</li>
      <li>Shortest-path traversal is run per target table under `maxJoinHops`.</li>
      <li>Resolved edges are merged without duplicates.</li>
      <li>Unresolved tables are captured and later enforced by AST validator.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 6 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["FK metadata via schema inspector (R)", "Graph vertex/edge construction."], ["semantic-layer relationships (R)", "Join expectations and hints."], ["ce_audit (W)", "JOIN_PATH_RESOLVED determinant."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">7</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>SemanticAstGenerationStage</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Generate strict JSON AST using LLM.

**Session Mutations:** `astRawJson`, `astVersion`, `SemanticQueryAstV1`, `canonicalAst`.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** `ce_config` prompt keys for `DefaultSemanticAstGenerator`, `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-7">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticAstGenerationStage.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/stage/provider/SemanticAstGenerationStage.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`AstGenerationResult generated = generator.generate(
  context.question(), context.retrieval(), context.joinPath(), context.session());
context.astGeneration(generated);
if (generated != null && generated.ast() != null) {
  context.canonicalAst(astCanonicalizer.fromV1(generated.ast()));
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSemanticAstGenerator.doGenerate()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/llm/DefaultSemanticAstGenerator.java">
{`String raw = llmClient.generateJsonStrict(session, llmPrompt, jsonSchema, ctxJson);
SemanticQueryAstV1 ast = mapper.readValue(raw, SemanticQueryAstV1.class);
ast = astNormalizer.normalize(ast, model, entity, session);
publishLlmEvent(ConvEngineAuditStage.AST_OUTPUT.name(), session, false, llmOutputPayload);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>Stage runs only after retrieval + join-path success.</li>
      <li>Prompt context includes question, selected entity, allowed entities, candidate tables, join path, and context json.</li>
      <li>Schema JSON is entity-specialized so generated fields stay within selected semantic entity.</li>
      <li>LLM output is strict JSON; SQL text output is not accepted in this stage.</li>
      <li>Raw JSON is normalized and audited via `AST_INPUT`, `AST_OUTPUT`, `AST_ERROR` determinants.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 7 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["ce_config (R)", "SYSTEM_PROMPT / USER_PROMPT / SCHEMA_PROMPT."], ["ce_audit (W)", "AST_INPUT / AST_OUTPUT / AST_ERROR."], ["ce_verbose (R)", "Verbose determinant labels."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">8</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>SemanticAstValidationStage</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Validate canonical AST against semantic contracts.

**Session Mutations:** `astValidation.valid`, `astValidation.errors`.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** semantic model fields/metrics/rules, `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-8">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticAstValidationStage.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/stage/provider/SemanticAstValidationStage.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`AstValidationResult result = validator.validate(
  context.canonicalAst(), model, context.joinPath(), context.session());
context.astValidation(result);
if (!result.valid()) {
  throw new IllegalStateException("semantic AST validation failed: " + result.errors());
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultAstValidator key checks" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/validate/DefaultAstValidator.java">
{`validateExistsBlocks(errors, ast.existsBlocks(), model);
validateSubqueryFilters(errors, ast.subqueryFilters(), fieldNames, model);
validateWindows(errors, ast.windows(), fieldNames);
if (ast.limit() > maxLimit) errors.add("limit exceeds max: " + ast.limit());`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>Entity must exist in semantic model; unknown entity fails immediately.</li>
      <li>Projection/group/sort/filter field keys are validated against semantic fields.</li>
      <li>Operator-value shape is validated (`IN`, `BETWEEN`, null-check operators, etc.).</li>
      <li>Exists/subquery/window clauses are recursively validated.</li>
      <li>Unresolved join-path tables and limit/offset constraints are enforced pre-compile.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 8 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["semantic-layer.yaml (R)", "Entity/field/operator/metric contract."], ["ce_audit (W)", "AST_VALIDATED determinant."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">9</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>SemanticSqlCompileStage</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Deterministic AST -> parameterized SQL compile + policy validation.

**Session Mutations:** `compiledSql`, `compiledSqlParams`, `sqlCompiled=true`.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** semantic model mappings, SQL clause/operator/window handlers, `McpSqlGuardrail`, `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-9">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticSqlCompileStage.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/stage/provider/SemanticSqlCompileStage.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`CompiledSql compiled = compiler.compile(context);
resolveValidator(context).validate(compiled, context);
context.compiledSql(compiled);
publishCompiled(context.session(), compiled);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSemanticSqlCompiler.compile()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/compiler/DefaultSemanticSqlCompiler.java">
{`CompileWorkPlan plan = new CompileWorkPlan(context, ast, model, entity, context.joinPath());
clauseHandlerRegistry.applyAll(plan);
return plan.getCompiledSql();`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSemanticSqlPolicyValidator.validate()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/policy/DefaultSemanticSqlPolicyValidator.java">
{`sqlGuardrail.assertReadOnly(compiledSql.sql(), "semantic.query");`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>Compile stage runs only after AST validation is successful.</li>
      <li>Compiler uses canonical AST and semantic model to resolve physical columns/tables.</li>
      <li>Clause handler registries apply predicates, metrics, windows, exists, and subqueries.</li>
      <li>Output SQL is always parameterized with named bind values.</li>
      <li>Policy validator applies read-only guardrail before execution stage.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 9 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["semantic-layer.yaml (R)", "Field-to-column and metric mappings."], ["ce_audit (W)", "SQL_COMPILED determinant."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">10</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>SemanticSqlExecuteStage</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Execute compiled SQL and map result rows.

**Session Mutations:** `execution.rowCount`, `execution.rows[]`, `_db.sql`, `_db.params`.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** datasource/JDBC, domain tables (read-only), `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-10">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticSqlExecuteStage.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/stage/provider/SemanticSqlExecuteStage.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`SemanticSqlExecutor executor = resolveExecutor(context);
SemanticExecutionResult result = executor.execute(context.compiledSql(), context);
context.executionResult(result);
publishExecuted(context, result);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSemanticSqlExecutor.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/execute/DefaultSemanticSqlExecutor.java">
{`List<Map<String, Object>> rows = jdbcTemplate.queryForList(
  compiledSql.sql(),
  compiledSql.params() == null ? Map.of() : compiledSql.params()
);
return new SemanticExecutionResult(rows.size(), List.copyOf(rows));`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>Stage fails fast if SQL compile output is missing.</li>
      <li>Named-parameter SQL executes through `NamedParameterJdbcTemplate`.</li>
      <li>Result rows are copied into immutable execution payload.</li>
      <li>Audit payload captures SQL and bind params under `_db` for debugging.</li>
      <li>DB grammar/type/permission errors are surfaced as `SQL_EXECUTE_ERROR` with root cause.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 10 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["zapper transactional tables (R)", "SELECT execution only."], ["ce_audit (W)", "SQL_EXECUTED/SQL_EXECUTE_ERROR."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">11</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>SemanticResultSummaryStage</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Build deterministic text/markdown summary from result rows.

**Session Mutations:** `summary`.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** execution result data, `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-11">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticResultSummaryStage.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/stage/provider/SemanticResultSummaryStage.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`SemanticResultSummarizer summarizer = resolveSummarizer(context);
String summary = summarizer.summarize(context.executionResult(), context);
context.summary(summary);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSemanticResultSummarizer.summarize()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/summary/DefaultSemanticResultSummarizer.java">
{`if (result.rowCount() == 0) return "No matching records found.";
return buildMarkdownTable(result);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>No-result branch returns deterministic string, not LLM-generated prose.</li>
      <li>Result-table branch extracts headers from first row keys.</li>
      <li>Rows are serialized as markdown table to render in ConvEngine UI/docs trace.</li>
      <li>Cell escape logic keeps table valid for symbols/newlines.</li>
      <li>Summary preview + length are emitted into audit payload.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 11 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["execution.rows (R)", "Summary source rows."], ["ce_audit (W)", "RESULT_SUMMARIZED."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">12</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>McpPlanner + RulesStep (POST_AGENT_MCP)</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Planner finalizes answer and rules complete post-MCP transitions.

**Session Mutations:** `mcp.finalAnswer`, outcome/status flags, state transitions.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** `ce_mcp_planner`, `ce_rule`, `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-12">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="McpToolStep ANSWER branch" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/steps/McpToolStep.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`if (McpConstants.ACTION_ANSWER.equalsIgnoreCase(plan.action())) {
  writeFinalAnswerToContext(session, plan.answer());
  session.putInputParam(ConvEngineInputParamKey.MCP_FINAL_ANSWER, plan.answer());
  break;
}`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="RulesStep.applyRules(...)" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/steps/RulesStep.java">
{`String phase = RulePhase.normalize(requestedPhase);
List<CeRule> allRules = staticCacheService.findEligibleRules(passIntent, passState, phase);
actionResolver.resolve(session, rule);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>After semantic execution, planner receives fresh observations and decides final answer text.</li>
      <li>`mcp.finalAnswer` is stored in context and input params.</li>
      <li>POST_AGENT_MCP rule phase runs to move workflow state.</li>
      <li>Rule actions can map to success/failure/reset states.</li>
      <li>Planner and rule outcomes are auditable for RCA.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 12 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["ce_mcp_planner (R)", "Answer synthesis prompt."], ["ce_rule (R)", "POST_AGENT_MCP transitions."], ["ce_audit (W)", "Planner + rule outcomes."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

<div className="ce-step-badge-list" role="list" style={{ marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
  <div className="ce-step-badge-item"><span className="ce-step-badge-index">13</span><span className="ce-step-badge-label" style={{ fontSize: '1.04rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>ResponseResolutionStep + Assistant output</span></div>
</div>

**Responsibility:** Resolve final response mapping and emit assistant payload.

**Session Mutations:** `OutputPayload` + persisted turn output.

**Config/Table Dependencies:** `ce_response`, `ce_prompt_template`, `ce_output_schema` (optional), `ce_conversation`, `ce_audit`.

<Tabs groupId="semantic-runtime-step-13">
  <TabItem value="code" label="Code" default>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="ResponseResolutionStep.execute()" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/steps/ResponseResolutionStep.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`Optional<CeResponse> responseOptional = resolveResponse(session);
CeResponse resp = responseOptional.get();
typeFactory.get(resp.getResponseType(), session)
  .resolve(session, PromptTemplate.initFrom(template), ResponseTemplate.initFrom(resp));`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
    <CodeBlockToggle title="ResponseResolutionStep assistant audit" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/steps/ResponseResolutionStep.java">
{`outputPayload.put(ConvEnginePayloadKey.OUTPUT, payloadValue);
outputPayload.put(ConvEnginePayloadKey.OUTPUT_FORMAT, resp.getOutputFormat());
audit.audit(ConvEngineAuditStage.ASSISTANT_OUTPUT, session.getConversationId(), outputPayload);`}
    </CodeBlockToggle>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="logic" label="Detailed Execution Logic">
    <ol>
      <li>Response row is selected by intent/state and priority.</li>
      <li>Response type handler renders EXACT/DERIVED payload accordingly.</li>
      <li>Output transformers are applied if configured.</li>
      <li>Final payload is attached to session and returned as assistant turn output.</li>
      <li>Assistant output determinant closes the turn-level audit trail.</li>
    </ol>
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="tables" label="Tables Involved">
    <DbTable title="Step 13 table touch points" columns={["Table / source", "Access pattern"]} rows={[["ce_response (R)", "Intent/state response mapping."], ["ce_prompt_template (R)", "Template rows for DERIVED/SCHEMA-based response."], ["ce_output_schema (R optional)", "Output schema helper context."], ["ce_conversation (W)", "Persisted final turn."], ["ce_audit (W)", "ASSISTANT_OUTPUT."]]} />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

</div>

## Semantic Model YAML (`semantic-layer.yaml`)

Semantic mode relies on a declarative semantic model file that maps business language to physical schema. Retrieval, AST validation, join-path planning, metric compilation, and guardrails all consume this file.

<DbTable
  title="YAML section ownership"
  columns={["Section", "Primary consumers", "Runtime effect"]}
  rows={[
    ["settings", "retrieval + compiler", "default limits, timezone, SQL dialect hints"],
    ["entities", "retrieval + validator + compiler", "business entities, synonyms, canonical fields"],
    ["tables", "graph/planner/compiler", "physical columns and foreign keys"],
    ["relationships", "join-path stage", "table traversal edges and cardinality hints"],
    ["join_hints", "planner/compiler", "frequent join relationships"],
    ["metrics", "validator + compiler", "allowed metric keys and SQL expressions"],
    ["value_patterns", "normalizer", "global value-prefix-driven field remap before validation/compile"],
    ["synonyms", "retrieval", "domain query vocabulary expansion"],
    ["rules", "policy/guardrail", "allowed tables, denied operations, max limit"]
  ]}
/>

<Highlight type="info" title="Configured path">
`mcp.db.semantic.model-path=classpath:/mcp/semantic-layer.yaml`
</Highlight>

### Complete sample semantic model

<CodeBlockToggle title="semantic-layer.yaml (full sample)" language="yaml" defaultOpen={true}>
{`version: 1
database: zapper_ops
description: >
  Semantic model for Zapper disconnect workflow analytics and production diagnostics.
  This model maps user/business language (disconnect, downstream failure, BillBank gap,
  account status) to physical database tables and join paths.

settings:
  default_limit: 100
  timezone: UTC
  sql_dialect: postgres

entities:
  Account:
    description: >
      Represents a Zapper customer billing account used as the anchor for request,
      order, and billing diagnostics.
    synonyms:
      - contract
      - subscription
      - service account
      - customer account
      - billing account
    example_questions:
      - show account details for UPSA100
      - what is account status for ACMA200
      - list accounts created this week
      - show billing cost for account UPSA100
    tables:
      primary: zp_account
      related:
        - zp_customer
    fields:
      accountId:
        column: zp_account.account_id
        type: string
        description: unique account identifier used across request/order/billing tables
        searchable: true
        filterable: true
        example: UPSA100
      customerId:
        column: zp_account.customer_id
        type: string
        description: owner customer identifier linked to zp_customer
        searchable: true
        filterable: true
      accountStatus:
        column: zp_account.account_status
        type: string
        description: account lifecycle status in Zapper
        filterable: true
        allowed_values:
          - ACTIVE
          - SUSPENDED
          - CLOSED
      currentBillingCost:
        column: zp_account.current_billing_cost
        type: number
        description: current computed billing cost amount for account
      createdAt:
        column: zp_account.created_at
        type: timestamp
        description: account creation timestamp

  DisconnectRequest:
    description: >
      Represents disconnect workflow requests and downstream order execution state.
      This is the main entity for "why disconnect failed" style analysis.
    synonyms:
      - disconnect
      - disconnection
      - service termination
      - cancel service
      - disconnect request
      - failed disconnect
    example_questions:
      - show failed disconnect requests last 24 hours
      - why disconnect failed for request ZPR1003
      - list disconnect requests for account UPSA100
      - show request status and downstream status together
      - find requests where disconnect id is missing
    tables:
      primary: zp_request
      related:
        - zp_disconnect_order
        - zp_order_downstream_check
        - zp_ui_data
    fields:
      requestId:
        column: zp_request.zp_request_id
        type: string
        key: true
        searchable: true
        filterable: true
        aliases:
          - id
          - request id
          - req id
        description: unique request id (example pattern ZPR*)
        example: ZPR1003
      accountId:
        column: zp_request.account_id
        type: string
        searchable: true
        filterable: true
        description: account associated with request
      requestStatus:
        column: zp_request.request_status
        type: string
        filterable: true
        aliases:
          - status
          - request state
        description: request-level status from orchestration layer
        allowed_values:
          - SUBMITTED
          - IN_PROGRESS
          - FAILED
          - COMPLETED
      requestedAt:
        column: zp_request.requested_at
        type: timestamp
        aliases:
          - created
          - created at
          - request time
        description: request timestamp used for time-window diagnostics
      disconnectOrderId:
        column: zp_disconnect_order.don
        type: string
        searchable: true
        filterable: true
        description: downstream disconnect order number (DON*)
        example: DON9001
      downstreamStatus:
        column: zp_disconnect_order.downstream_status
        type: string
        filterable: true
        description: downstream orchestration status for disconnect order
        allowed_values:
          - COMPLETED
          - FAILED
          - PENDING
          - INVENTORY_ERROR
      disconnectId:
        column: zp_disconnect_order.zp_disconnect_id
        type: string
        searchable: true
        filterable: true
        description: generated disconnect identifier, can be null during failures
      teamNotes:
        column: zp_ui_data.zp_asr_team_notes
        type: string
        description: latest operations team note useful for RCA context
      failureReason:
        column: zp_ui_data.zp_asr_team_notes
        type: string
        filterable: true
        searchable: true
        description: normalized failure-reason view for request-level RCA prompts

  DownstreamCheck:
    description: >
      Represents validation checks executed in downstream disconnect flow.
      Used to diagnose which specific check failed and why.
    synonyms:
      - check
      - validation check
      - downstream validation
      - downstream rule
      - check failure
    example_questions:
      - list failed checks for DON9001
      - which check failed for request ZPR1003
      - show failure reason for request ZPR1003
      - show downstream validation failures last 24 hours
    tables:
      primary: zp_order_downstream_check
      related:
        - zp_disconnect_order
    fields:
      checkId:
        column: zp_order_downstream_check.check_id
        type: string
        key: true
        searchable: true
        description: unique check record identifier
      disconnectOrderId:
        column: zp_order_downstream_check.don
        type: string
        filterable: true
        searchable: true
        description: disconnect order linked to this check
      requestId:
        column: zp_disconnect_order.zp_request_id
        type: string
        filterable: true
        searchable: true
        description: request id associated with this downstream check via disconnect order
      checkCode:
        column: zp_order_downstream_check.check_code
        type: string
        filterable: true
        description: business check code executed downstream
      checkStatus:
        column: zp_order_downstream_check.check_status
        type: string
        filterable: true
        description: result of downstream validation check
        allowed_values:
          - PASSED
          - FAILED
          - SKIPPED
      failureReason:
        column: zp_order_downstream_check.failure_reason
        type: string
        description: captured failure reason when checkStatus=FAILED
      checkedAt:
        column: zp_order_downstream_check.checked_at
        type: timestamp
        description: time check was executed

  BillingRecord:
    description: >
      Represents BillBank/billing records associated with disconnect outcomes.
      Used to identify billing reconciliation gaps after disconnect.
    synonyms:
      - billing
      - billbank
      - invoice
      - bill record
      - billing reconciliation
    example_questions:
      - show billbank record for disconnect id ZPDISC1001
      - list pending billing records for account UPSA100
      - find disconnects missing billbank record
    tables:
      primary: zp_billbank_record
      related:
        - zp_disconnect_order
    fields:
      billbankId:
        column: zp_billbank_record.billbank_id
        type: string
        key: true
        searchable: true
        description: BillBank record identifier
      accountId:
        column: zp_billbank_record.account_id
        type: string
        filterable: true
        searchable: true
        description: account tied to billing record
      disconnectId:
        column: zp_billbank_record.zp_disconnect_id
        type: string
        filterable: true
        searchable: true
        description: disconnect identifier linked to billing record
      recordStatus:
        column: zp_billbank_record.record_status
        type: string
        filterable: true
        description: BillBank processing status
        allowed_values:
          - POSTED
          - PENDING
          - FAILED
      pendingBillAmount:
        column: zp_billbank_record.pending_bill_amount
        type: number
        description: pending bill amount for account/disconnect
      updatedAt:
        column: zp_billbank_record.updated_at
        type: timestamp
        description: record last update timestamp

tables:
  zp_account:
    description: account master data
    columns:
      account_id:
        type: varchar
        primary_key: true
        description: unique account identifier
      customer_id:
        type: varchar
        description: customer owner id
        foreign_key:
          table: zp_customer
          column: customer_id
      account_status:
        type: varchar
        description: account lifecycle status
      current_billing_cost:
        type: numeric
        description: current billing amount
      created_at:
        type: timestamptz
        description: account creation time

  zp_customer:
    description: customer master data
    columns:
      customer_id:
        type: varchar
        primary_key: true
      customer_name:
        type: varchar

  zp_request:
    description: disconnect request master table
    columns:
      zp_request_id:
        type: varchar
        primary_key: true
      account_id:
        type: varchar
        foreign_key:
          table: zp_account
          column: account_id
      request_status:
        type: varchar
      requested_at:
        type: timestamptz

  zp_disconnect_order:
    description: downstream disconnect order tracking
    columns:
      don:
        type: varchar
        primary_key: true
      zp_request_id:
        type: varchar
        foreign_key:
          table: zp_request
          column: zp_request_id
      account_id:
        type: varchar
        foreign_key:
          table: zp_account
          column: account_id
      downstream_status:
        type: varchar
      zp_disconnect_id:
        type: varchar

  zp_order_downstream_check:
    description: downstream validation checks
    columns:
      check_id:
        type: varchar
        primary_key: true
      don:
        type: varchar
        foreign_key:
          table: zp_disconnect_order
          column: don
      check_code:
        type: varchar
      check_status:
        type: varchar
      failure_reason:
        type: varchar
      checked_at:
        type: timestamptz

  zp_ui_data:
    description: latest UI operations notes per request
    columns:
      zp_request_id:
        type: varchar
        primary_key: true
        foreign_key:
          table: zp_request
          column: zp_request_id
      zp_asr_team_notes:
        type: varchar

  zp_billbank_record:
    description: bill-bank records for disconnect and cease state
    columns:
      billbank_id:
        type: varchar
        primary_key: true
      account_id:
        type: varchar
        foreign_key:
          table: zp_account
          column: account_id
      zp_disconnect_id:
        type: varchar
      record_status:
        type: varchar
      pending_bill_amount:
        type: numeric
      updated_at:
        type: timestamptz

relationships:
  - name: account_to_request
    description: an account can have many disconnect requests
    from:
      table: zp_account
      column: account_id
    to:
      table: zp_request
      column: account_id
    type: one_to_many

  - name: request_to_disconnect_order
    description: request to downstream disconnect order
    from:
      table: zp_request
      column: zp_request_id
    to:
      table: zp_disconnect_order
      column: zp_request_id
    type: one_to_many

  - name: request_to_ui_data
    description: request to latest UI note payload
    from:
      table: zp_request
      column: zp_request_id
    to:
      table: zp_ui_data
      column: zp_request_id
    type: one_to_one

  - name: disconnect_order_to_check
    description: disconnect order to downstream checks
    from:
      table: zp_disconnect_order
      column: don
    to:
      table: zp_order_downstream_check
      column: don
    type: one_to_many

  - name: account_to_billbank
    description: account to billbank records
    from:
      table: zp_account
      column: account_id
    to:
      table: zp_billbank_record
      column: account_id
    type: one_to_many

  - name: disconnect_to_billbank
    description: disconnect id mapped to billbank records when generated
    from:
      table: zp_disconnect_order
      column: zp_disconnect_id
    to:
      table: zp_billbank_record
      column: zp_disconnect_id
    type: one_to_many

synonyms:
  account:
    - contract
    - subscription
    - billing account
    - customer account
  disconnect:
    - service termination
    - cancel service
    - disconnection
    - cease service
  downstream:
    - order check
    - validation
    - orchestration
  billing:
    - billbank
    - invoice
    - reconciliation

join_hints:
  zp_request:
    commonly_joined_with:
      - zp_disconnect_order
      - zp_ui_data
      - zp_account
      - zp_order_downstream_check

  zp_disconnect_order:
    commonly_joined_with:
      - zp_request
      - zp_order_downstream_check
      - zp_billbank_record

metrics:
  failed_disconnect_count:
    description: count of disconnect requests with non-completed downstream status
    sql: |
      COUNT(CASE WHEN zp_disconnect_order.downstream_status NOT IN ('COMPLETED') THEN 1 END)

  pending_disconnect_count:
    description: count of disconnect requests still pending downstream completion
    sql: |
      COUNT(CASE WHEN zp_disconnect_order.downstream_status IN ('PENDING') THEN 1 END)

  billbank_gap_count:
    description: count of disconnect orders missing billbank linkage
    sql: |
      COUNT(CASE WHEN zp_disconnect_order.zp_disconnect_id IS NOT NULL
                 AND zp_billbank_record.zp_disconnect_id IS NULL THEN 1 END)

value_patterns:
  - from_field: requestId
    to_field: disconnectOrderId
    value_starts_with: [DON]
  - from_field: disconnectOrderId
    to_field: requestId
    value_starts_with: [ZPR]

intent_rules:
  don_failure_reason_details:
    description: stabilize DON-level failure asks to disconnect-order diagnostics output
    match_any: [why did, fail, failed, failure reason]
    must_contain: [don]
    force_entity: DisconnectRequest
    force_mode: detail
    force_select: [disconnectOrderId, downstreamStatus, failureReason, requestId]

  request_failure_reason_details:
    description: stabilize request-level failure-reason asks to request diagnostics output
    match_any: [failure reason, reason for request, why request failed, failed reason]
    must_contain: [request]
    force_entity: DisconnectRequest
    force_mode: detail
    force_select: [requestId, failureReason]

  billbank_gap_details:
    description: force billbank gap details flow
    match_any: [billbank gap, billbank gaps, billing gap, billing gaps]
    must_contain: [request, order, detail]
    force_entity: DisconnectRequest
    force_mode: detail
    force_mode_even_with_metrics: true
    force_select: [requestId, accountId, requestStatus, requestedAt, disconnectOrderId, downstreamStatus, disconnectId, teamNotes]
    enforce_where:
      - field: disconnectId
        op: IS_NULL
        value: null

rules:
  allowed_tables:
    - zp_account
    - zp_customer
    - zp_request
    - zp_disconnect_order
    - zp_order_downstream_check
    - zp_ui_data
    - zp_billbank_record
  deny_operations:
    - DELETE
    - UPDATE
    - DROP
  max_result_limit: 500`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

## `semantic-layer.yaml`

This section explains every major tag in the full sample and what ConvEngine actually does with it at runtime.

<Highlight type="info" title="Important runtime behavior">
`SemanticModelLoader` is configured with `FAIL_ON_UNKNOWN_PROPERTIES=false`.  
That means unknown/unmapped YAML tags are ignored safely at load time.
</Highlight>

<DbTable
  title="Top-level tag behavior"
  columns={["Tag", "Loaded into model", "Runtime effect", "Primary code path"]}
  rows={[
    ["version", "Yes", "Returned in output/audit as semanticModelVersion.", "model/SemanticModel, runtime/core/SemanticQueryRuntimeService"],
    ["database", "Yes", "Informational model identity.", "model/SemanticModel"],
    ["description", "Yes", "Used as descriptive context only.", "model/SemanticModel"],
    ["entities", "Yes", "Core retrieval + AST schema specialization + field validation + SQL compile mapping.", "retrieval/*, llm/DefaultSemanticAstGenerator, ast/validate/DefaultAstValidator, sql/*"],
    ["tables", "Yes", "Schema graph and model validation for physical table references.", "model/SemanticModelValidator, graph/*"],
    ["relationships", "Yes", "Join-path planning and correlation predicates.", "graph/provider/DefaultJoinPathResolver, sql/handler/clause/*"],
    ["metrics", "Yes", "Allowed metric keys and SQL expressions in aggregate queries.", "llm/DefaultSemanticAstGenerator, ast/validate/DefaultAstValidator, sql/handler/clause/*"],
    ["value_patterns", "Yes", "Global value-prefix remap rules applied before validation/compile (example DON* from requestId to disconnectOrderId).", "ast/normalize/DefaultAstNormalizer"],
    ["intent_rules", "Yes", "Deterministic query-intent overrides (entity/mode/select/filters) applied during AST normalization.", "ast/normalize/DefaultAstNormalizer"],
    ["synonyms", "Yes (top-level map)", "Currently loaded; retrieval mainly uses entity-level synonyms.", "model/SemanticModel, retrieval/provider/DefaultSemanticEntityTableRetriever"],
    ["settings", "No (ignored currently)", "No direct runtime effect from YAML tag itself; limits/timezone come from application config.", "config/ConvEngineMcpConfig"],
    ["join_hints", "No (ignored currently)", "No direct runtime effect from YAML tag currently.", "N/A (ignored by loader)"],
    ["rules", "No (ignored currently)", "No direct runtime effect from YAML tag currently.", "N/A (ignored by loader)"]
  ]}
/>

### 1) Model identity tags

<CodeBlockToggle title="Snippet: model identity" language="yaml" defaultOpen={false}>
{`version: 1
database: zapper_ops
description: Semantic model for Zapper disconnect workflow analytics.`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What this does:
- `version`: surfaces as `semanticModelVersion` in runtime output and stage payloads.
- `database` + `description`: metadata/context only; not a SQL generator by itself.

### 2) `entities` block

<CodeBlockToggle title="Snippet: one entity contract" language="yaml" defaultOpen={false}>
{`entities:
  DisconnectRequest:
    description: Main disconnect workflow entity
    synonyms: [disconnect, disconnection, service termination]
    tables:
      primary: zp_request
      related: [zp_disconnect_order, zp_order_downstream_check, zp_ui_data]
    fields:
      requestId:
        column: zp_request.zp_request_id
        type: string
        key: true
        searchable: true
        filterable: true
      teamNotes:
        column: zp_ui_data.zp_asr_team_notes
        type: string
      failureReason:
        column: zp_ui_data.zp_asr_team_notes
        type: string`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

How each child tag is used:

<DbTable
  title="Entity tag behavior"
  columns={["Tag", "Used by", "Effect on AST/SQL"]}
  rows={[
    ["entities.<name>", "retrieval + validator", "Becomes candidate entity and AST entity target."],
    ["description", "retrieval + LLM prompt", "Improves retrieval relevance and LLM grounding context."],
    ["synonyms", "retrieval (+ embedding text)", "Raises deterministic synonym score for candidate ranking."],
    ["tables.primary", "planner/compiler/validator", "Primary base table candidate for joins and projections."],
    ["tables.related", "retrieval/planner", "Expands table candidates for join-path resolution."],
    ["fields.<fieldName>.column", "compiler", "Maps semantic field key to physical table.column in SQL select/where/order/group."],
    ["fields.<fieldName>.type", "validator", "Operator/type validation (e.g., ILIKE requires string-like field)."],
    ["fields.<fieldName>.description", "retrieval", "Extra lexical signal for entity/field matching."],
    ["fields.<fieldName>.aliases", "normalizer + LLM prompt context", "Maps user/LLM variants (for example id/status/created) to canonical semantic field keys."],
    ["fields.<fieldName>.filterable/searchable/key", "currently metadata", "Carried in model; not strict query gating in current validator/compiler."]
  ]}
/>

Example:
- User asks: `show requests where teamNotes contains billing`
- Retrieval picks `DisconnectRequest` (field ownership + lexical/synonym/vector signals).
- AST schema specialization restricts allowed field keys for selected entity.
- Compiler uses `teamNotes -> zp_ui_data.zp_asr_team_notes` and, if filters reference another table-owned field (for example `requestId -> zp_request.zp_request_id`), compile stage auto-expands required tables and adds the join path.

### 3) `tables` + `columns` + `foreign_key`

<CodeBlockToggle title="Snippet: physical table dictionary" language="yaml" defaultOpen={false}>
{`tables:
  zp_request:
    description: disconnect request master table
    columns:
      zp_request_id:
        type: varchar
        primary_key: true
      account_id:
        type: varchar
        foreign_key:
          table: zp_account
          column: account_id
      request_status:
        type: varchar
      requested_at:
        type: timestamptz`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What this does:
- Provides table/column metadata for schema validation and graph wiring.
- `primary_key` and `foreign_key` are model-level structure hints.
- `foreign_key.table/column` can contribute to relationship sanity and graph traversal completeness.

### 4) `relationships`

<CodeBlockToggle title="Snippet: relationship edge" language="yaml" defaultOpen={false}>
{`relationships:
  - name: request_to_disconnect_order
    description: request to downstream disconnect order
    from: { table: zp_request, column: zp_request_id }
    to:   { table: zp_disconnect_order, column: zp_request_id }
    type: one_to_many`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What this does:
- Join-path stage builds traversal edges from these mappings.
- SQL compiler uses edges to generate deterministic joins.
- Correlation predicates for EXISTS/subqueries also rely on relationship knowledge.

### 5) `metrics`

<CodeBlockToggle title="Snippet: metric definition" language="yaml" defaultOpen={false}>
{`metrics:
  billbank_gap_count:
    description: count of disconnect orders missing billbank linkage
    sql: |
      COUNT(CASE WHEN zp_disconnect_order.zp_disconnect_id IS NOT NULL
                 AND zp_billbank_record.zp_disconnect_id IS NULL THEN 1 END)`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What this does:
- Metric key becomes allowed value in AST `metrics[]`.
- Metric SQL is inserted by compiler when aggregation is requested.
- Having clause can reference metric keys.

Critical rule:
- If `metrics` is present with detail projections, selected fields must be grouped (`group_by`) or query is invalid.

### 6) `synonyms` (top-level)

<CodeBlockToggle title="Snippet: top-level synonyms map" language="yaml" defaultOpen={false}>
{`synonyms:
  disconnect: [service termination, disconnection]
  billing: [billbank, invoice, reconciliation]`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

Current behavior:
- Loaded into model and available for future expansion.
- Main retrieval scoring today relies primarily on entity-level synonyms + fields + descriptions.

### 7) `value_patterns` + `intent_rules` (deterministic bridge for ambiguous asks)

<CodeBlockToggle title="Snippet: intent rule for billbank gap details" language="yaml" defaultOpen={false}>
{`value_patterns:
  - from_field: requestId
    to_field: disconnectOrderId
    value_starts_with: [DON]
  - from_field: disconnectOrderId
    to_field: requestId
    value_starts_with: [ZPR]

intent_rules:
  don_failure_reason_details:
    description: stabilize DON-level failure asks to disconnect-order diagnostics output
    match_any: [why did, fail, failed, failure reason]
    must_contain: [don]
    force_entity: DisconnectRequest
    force_mode: detail
    force_select: [disconnectOrderId, downstreamStatus, failureReason, requestId]

  request_failure_reason_details:
    description: stabilize request-level failure-reason asks to request diagnostics output
    match_any: [failure reason, reason for request, why request failed, failed reason]
    must_contain: [request]
    force_entity: DisconnectRequest
    force_mode: detail
    force_select: [requestId, failureReason]

  billbank_gap_details:
    description: force billbank gap details flow
    match_any: [billbank gap, billbank gaps, billing gap, billing gaps]
    must_contain: [request, order, detail]
    force_entity: DisconnectRequest
    force_mode: detail
    force_mode_even_with_metrics: true
    force_select: [requestId, accountId, requestStatus, requestedAt, disconnectOrderId, downstreamStatus, disconnectId, teamNotes]
    enforce_where:
      - field: disconnectId
        op: IS_NULL
        value: null`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What this does at runtime:
- `match_any` + `must_contain` gates when rule activates.
- `force_entity` overrides LLM-selected entity.
- `force_mode: detail` drops accidental aggregate pieces (`metrics`, `having`, `group_by`).
- `force_mode_even_with_metrics: true` allows this rule to force detail/select even if AST contains `metrics`.
- `force_select` sets deterministic projection for that business intent.
- `enforce_where` injects deterministic filters.
- Global `value_patterns` applies deterministic filter-field remap based on value prefix (example `requestId + DON* -> disconnectOrderId`) without hardcoding in framework.
- Rule-level `field_remaps` is still supported for rule-specific overrides when needed.

<Highlight type="info" title="Latest Contract Changes">
`SemanticField` supports optional `aliases` in YAML. `SemanticModel` supports top-level `value_patterns` (global remaps), and `SemanticIntentRule` supports optional `field_remaps` (rule-specific remaps), all mapped via `SemanticIntentFieldRemap`.
</Highlight>

### 8) `settings`, `join_hints`, `rules`, and other descriptive tags

<CodeBlockToggle title="Snippet: currently ignored-by-loader tags" language="yaml" defaultOpen={false}>
{`settings:
  default_limit: 100
  timezone: UTC
  sql_dialect: postgres

join_hints:
  zp_request:
    commonly_joined_with: [zp_disconnect_order, zp_ui_data]

rules:
  allowed_tables: [zp_request, zp_disconnect_order]
  deny_operations: [DELETE, UPDATE, DROP]
  max_result_limit: 500`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

Current status:
- These tags are excellent documentation for model authors.
- They are not currently bound to `SemanticModel` records, so runtime ignores them.
- Effective runtime limit/timezone/dialect come from `application.yml` (`convengine.mcp.db.semantic.*`).
- DML/DDL guardrails are enforced by SQL policy/guardrail steps, not YAML `rules`.

Other descriptive tags in sample:
- `example_questions`, `allowed_values`, `example` are currently prompt/documentation aids and are not strict runtime-enforced model fields.

## AST + SQL impact walkthrough

User question:
- `show billbank gaps with request and order details`

LLM generated AST (problem shape):

<CodeBlockToggle title="Invalid mixed AST (detail + metric)" language="json" defaultOpen={false}>
{`{
  "entity": "BillingRecord",
  "select": ["billbankId","accountId","disconnectId","recordStatus","pendingBillAmount","updatedAt"],
  "group_by": [],
  "metrics": ["billbank_gap_count"],
  "having": {
    "op": "AND",
    "conditions": [{"field":"billbank_gap_count","op":">","value":0}],
    "groups": []
  }
}`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

Why validator rejects:
- Metrics + detailed select fields requires grouping.
- With empty `group_by`, SQL semantics are invalid.

With current normalizer fix:
- Mixed aggregate/detail AST is demoted to detail query.
- `metrics/having/group_by` are removed deterministically before validation.

<CodeBlockToggle title="Normalized AST after fix (detail mode)" language="json" defaultOpen={false}>
{`{
  "entity": "BillingRecord",
  "select": ["billbankId","accountId","disconnectId","recordStatus","pendingBillAmount","updatedAt"],
  "group_by": [],
  "metrics": [],
  "having": {"op":"AND","conditions":[],"groups":[]}
}`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

Typical SQL shape after fix:

<CodeBlockToggle title="Compiled SQL shape (detail mode)" language="sql" defaultOpen={false}>
{`select
  t0.billbank_id as billbankId,
  t0.account_id as accountId,
  t0.zp_disconnect_id as disconnectId,
  t0.record_status as recordStatus,
  t0.pending_bill_amount as pendingBillAmount,
  t0.updated_at as updatedAt
from zp_billbank_record t0
limit :__limit`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

If you want aggregate output intentionally, prompt explicitly:
- `show billbank gap count by accountId`

## Semantic Query Tool Runtime Deep Dive

This section explains the runtime tool path that starts at `db.semantic.query` and executes retrieval -> join path -> AST -> SQL -> summary in deterministic stage order.

<Highlight type="info" title="Exact source">
Runtime files below show how the semantic tool call is orchestrated from handler entry to summarized result.
</Highlight>

### High-level code execution order (runtime)

#### `DbSemanticQueryToolHandler.java`

<div className="ce-ast-backlink-wrap">
  <a className="ce-ast-backlink" href="#high-level-code-execution-order-runtime" title="Back to runtime execution order" aria-label="Back to runtime execution order">
    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12 5l-5 5h3v7h4v-7h3l-5-5zM5 19h14v2H5z" fill="currentColor"/></svg>

<CodeBlockToggle title="DbSemanticQueryToolHandler.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/handler/DbSemanticQueryToolHandler.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DbSemanticQueryToolHandler.java
// Purpose: MCP tool handler entrypoint for semantic query execution.
// Flow 1: Accepts tool args and extracts the semantic question payload.
// Flow 2: Delegates planning/execution to SemanticQueryRuntimeService.
// Flow 3: Returns normalized tool result envelope to MCP step.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.handler;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.core.*;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.config.ConvEngineMcpConfig;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.executor.adapter.DbToolHandler;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.session.EngineSession;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.entity.CeMcpTool;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.condition.ConditionalOnProperty;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.Map;

@Component
@RequiredArgsConstructor
@ConditionalOnProperty(prefix = "convengine.mcp.db.semantic", name = "enabled", havingValue = "true")
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DbSemanticQueryToolHandler implements DbToolHandler {

    private final ConvEngineMcpConfig mcpConfig;
    private final SemanticQueryRuntimeService runtimeService;

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String toolCode() {
        ConvEngineMcpConfig.Db.Semantic cfg = mcpConfig.getDb() == null ? new ConvEngineMcpConfig.Db.Semantic() : mcpConfig.getDb().getSemantic();
        return cfg.getToolCode() == null || cfg.getToolCode().isBlank() ? "db.semantic.query" : cfg.getToolCode();
    }

    @Override
// Executes core stage/operation logic and mutates shared context/state.
    public Object execute(CeMcpTool tool, Map<String, Object> args, EngineSession session) {
        String question = extractQuestion(args, session);
        return runtimeService.plan(question, session);
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private String extractQuestion(Map<String, Object> args, EngineSession session) {
        if (args != null) {
            Object query = args.get("question");
            if (query == null) {
                query = args.get("query");
            }
            if (query == null) {
                query = args.get("user_input");
            }
            if (query != null && !String.valueOf(query).isBlank()) {
                return String.valueOf(query);
            }
        }
        return session == null ? "" : session.getUserText();
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: MCP tool handler entrypoint for semantic query execution.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Receives db.semantic.query tool args, delegates to runtime service, and returns structured semantic result envelope.
  - 2) Integrates with stage audit trail and deterministic runtime transitions.

// Purpose: Stage lifecycle extension contract.
// Flow 1: Defines before/after/onError hooks around each runtime stage.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.core;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.session.EngineSession;

// Primary type declaration for this component.
public interface SemanticQueryStageInterceptor {

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    default boolean supports(EngineSession session) {
        return true;
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    default void beforeStage(String stage, EngineSession session, Object payload) {
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    default void afterStage(String stage, EngineSession session, Object payload) {
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    default void onError(String stage, EngineSession session, Exception ex) {
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Provides before/after/error hooks around each semantic runtime stage for extension and audit customization.
