<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSubqueryClauseHandler.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/clause/provider/DefaultSubqueryClauseHandler.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DefaultSubqueryClauseHandler.java
// Purpose: Default subquery clause renderer.
// Flow 1: Compiles nested subqueries and binds nested params.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.clause.provider;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstOperator;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalSubqueryFilter;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalSubquerySpec;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticEntity;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticField;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.core.CompileWorkPlan;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.clause.core.AstSubqueryHandler;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.jooq.Condition;
import org.jooq.Field;
import org.jooq.impl.DSL;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;

@Component
@Order()
@RequiredArgsConstructor
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DefaultSubqueryClauseHandler implements AstSubqueryHandler {

    private final DefaultPredicateClauseHandler predicateClauseHandler;

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public boolean supports(CompileWorkPlan plan) {
        return plan != null && plan.getQuery() != null && plan.getAst() != null;
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public void apply(CompileWorkPlan plan) {
        if (plan.getAst().subqueryFilters() == null || plan.getAst().subqueryFilters().isEmpty()) {
            return;
        }
        List<Condition> conditions = new ArrayList<>();
        for (CanonicalSubqueryFilter filter : plan.getAst().subqueryFilters()) {
            Condition c = toSubqueryFilterCondition(filter, plan);
            if (c != null) {
                conditions.add(c);
            }
        }
        if (!conditions.isEmpty()) {
            plan.getQuery().addConditions(conditions);
        }
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private Condition toSubqueryFilterCondition(CanonicalSubqueryFilter filter, CompileWorkPlan plan) {
        if (filter == null || filter.field() == null || filter.field().isBlank() || filter.subquery() == null) {
            return null;
        }
        Field<Object> outerField = predicateClauseHandler.resolveEntityField(plan.getEntity(), filter.field(), plan.getAliasByTable());
        if (outerField == null) {
            return null;
        }
        String subquerySql = buildScalarSubquerySql(filter.subquery(), plan);
        if (subquerySql.isBlank()) {
            return null;
        }
        AstOperator op = Objects.requireNonNullElse(filter.operator(), AstOperator.EQ);
        String token = switch (op) {
            case EQ -> "=";
            case NE -> "<>";
            case GT -> ">";
            case GTE -> ">=";
            case LT -> "<";
            case LTE -> "<=";
            default -> "=";
        };
        return DSL.condition("{0} " + token + " (" + subquerySql + ")", outerField);
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private String buildScalarSubquerySql(CanonicalSubquerySpec spec, CompileWorkPlan plan) {
        if (spec == null || spec.entity() == null || spec.selectField() == null) {
            return "";
        }
        SemanticEntity subEntity = plan.getModel().entities().get(spec.entity());
        if (subEntity == null || subEntity.tables() == null || subEntity.tables().primary() == null) {
            return "";
        }
        String subTable = subEntity.tables().primary();
        String subAlias = "sq" + plan.getParamIdx()[0];
        SemanticField select = subEntity.fields().get(spec.selectField());
        if (select == null || select.column() == null || select.column().isBlank()) {
            return "";
        }
        Field<Object> selectField = columnField(select.column(), Map.of(subTable, subAlias));
        StringBuilder sql = new StringBuilder("SELECT ").append(selectField)
                .append(" FROM ").append(subTable).append(" ").append(subAlias);
        List<String> wherePredicates = new ArrayList<>();
        String correlation = predicateClauseHandler.buildCorrelationPredicate(
                plan.getEntity(), plan.getAliasByTable(), subEntity, subAlias, plan.getModel());
        if (!correlation.isBlank()) {
            wherePredicates.add(correlation);
        }
        String whereSql = predicateClauseHandler.renderFilterGroupSql(
                spec.where(), subEntity, Map.of(subTable, subAlias), plan.getParams(), plan.getParamIdx(), plan.getModel());
        if (!whereSql.isBlank()) {
            wherePredicates.add(whereSql);
        }
        if (!wherePredicates.isEmpty()) {
            sql.append(" WHERE ").append(String.join(" AND ", wherePredicates));
        }
        if (spec.groupBy() != null && !spec.groupBy().isEmpty()) {
            List<String> group = new ArrayList<>();
            for (String fieldName : spec.groupBy()) {
                SemanticField field = subEntity.fields().get(fieldName);
                if (field != null && field.column() != null && !field.column().isBlank()) {
                    group.add(columnField(field.column(), Map.of(subTable, subAlias)).toString());
                }
            }
            if (!group.isEmpty()) {
                sql.append(" GROUP BY ").append(String.join(", ", group));
            }
        }
        String havingSql = predicateClauseHandler.renderFilterGroupSql(
                spec.having(), subEntity, Map.of(subTable, subAlias), plan.getParams(), plan.getParamIdx(), plan.getModel());
        if (!havingSql.isBlank()) {
            sql.append(" HAVING ").append(havingSql);
        }
        sql.append(" LIMIT ").append(Math.max(spec.limit(), 1));
        return sql.toString();
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private Field<Object> columnField(String tableDotColumn, Map<String, String> aliasByTable) {
        String[] parts = tableDotColumn.split("\\.");
        if (parts.length != 2) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Invalid semantic field column format: " + tableDotColumn);
        }
        String alias = aliasByTable.getOrDefault(parts[0], parts[0]);
        return DSL.field(DSL.name(alias, parts[1]));
    }
}

`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Default subquery clause implementation.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Renders nested select fragments and binds nested params safely.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

// Purpose: Registry for function handlers.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.clause.registry;

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstOperatorHandlerRegistry.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/operator/core/AstOperatorHandlerRegistry.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// AstOperatorHandlerRegistry.java
// Purpose: Operator renderer registry.
// Flow 1: Selects appropriate operator handler per operator/value shape.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstOperator;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.AnnotationAwareOrderComparator;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

@Component
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class AstOperatorHandlerRegistry {
    private final List<AstOperatorHandler> handlers;

    public AstOperatorHandlerRegistry(List<AstOperatorHandler> handlers) {
        List<AstOperatorHandler> sorted = new ArrayList<>(handlers == null ? List.of() : handlers);
        AnnotationAwareOrderComparator.sort(sorted);
        this.handlers = List.copyOf(sorted);
    }

// Resolves runtime strategy/handler/value using current semantic context.
    public AstOperatorHandler resolve(AstOperator operator) {
        if (operator == null) {
            return null;
        }
        for (AstOperatorHandler handler : handlers) {
            if (handler.supports(operator)) {
                return handler;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String sqlToken(AstOperator operator) {
        AstOperatorHandler handler = resolve(operator);
        return handler == null ? null : handler.sqlToken(operator);
    }
}

`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Operator handler registry.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Selects appropriate operator renderer by operator type and value shape.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

#### `OperatorHandlerContext.java`

<div className="ce-ast-backlink-wrap">

<CodeBlockToggle title="OperatorHandlerContext.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/operator/core/OperatorHandlerContext.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// OperatorHandlerContext.java
// Purpose: Operator rendering context model.
// Flow 1: Carries field metadata, params map, and plan state.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core;

import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.jooq.Param;
import org.jooq.impl.DSL;

import java.util.Map;
import java.util.function.Function;

@RequiredArgsConstructor
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class OperatorHandlerContext {
    private final Map<String, Object> params;
    private final int[] paramIdx;
    private final Function<Object, Object> normalizer;

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String nextParamKey(Object rawValue) {
        String key = "p" + paramIdx[0]++;
        params.put(key, normalize(rawValue));
        return key;
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public Param<Object> nextParam(Object rawValue) {
        String key = nextParamKey(rawValue);
        return DSL.param(key, params.get(key));
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public Object normalize(Object rawValue) {
        return normalizer == null ? rawValue : normalizer.apply(rawValue);
    }
}

`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Operator rendering context object.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Carries field mapping, params map, and compile plan state for operator handlers.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultComparisonAstOperatorHandler.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/operator/provider/DefaultComparisonAstOperatorHandler.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DefaultComparisonAstOperatorHandler.java
// Purpose: Comparison/LIKE/ILIKE operator renderer.
// Flow 1: Renders EQ/NE/GT/GTE/LT/LTE/LIKE/ILIKE operators.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.provider;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstOperator;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core.AstOperatorHandler;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core.OperatorHandlerContext;
import org.jooq.Condition;
import org.jooq.Field;
import org.jooq.impl.DSL;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.EnumSet;
import java.util.Set;

@Component
@Order()
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DefaultComparisonAstOperatorHandler implements AstOperatorHandler {
    private static final Set<AstOperator> SUPPORTED = EnumSet.of(
            AstOperator.EQ, AstOperator.NE, AstOperator.GT, AstOperator.GTE,
            AstOperator.LT, AstOperator.LTE, AstOperator.LIKE, AstOperator.ILIKE
    );

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public boolean supports(AstOperator operator) {
        return operator != null && SUPPORTED.contains(operator);
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public Condition buildCondition(Field<Object> field, Object value, AstOperator operator, OperatorHandlerContext context) {
        Object effectiveValue = normalizePatternValue(value, operator);
        return DSL.condition("{0} " + sqlToken(operator) + " {1}", field, context.nextParam(effectiveValue));
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String buildSql(Field<Object> field, Object value, AstOperator operator, OperatorHandlerContext context) {
        Object effectiveValue = normalizePatternValue(value, operator);
        String key = context.nextParamKey(effectiveValue);
        return field + " " + sqlToken(operator) + " :" + key;
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String sqlToken(AstOperator operator) {
        return switch (operator) {
            case EQ -> "=";
            case NE -> "<>";
            case GT -> ">";
            case GTE -> ">=";
            case LT -> "<";
            case LTE -> "<=";
            case LIKE -> "LIKE";
            case ILIKE -> "ILIKE";
            default -> null;
        };
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private Object normalizePatternValue(Object value, AstOperator operator) {
        if ((operator == AstOperator.LIKE || operator == AstOperator.ILIKE) && value instanceof String s) {
            if (!s.contains("%") && !s.contains("_")) {
                return "%" + s + "%";
            }
        }
        return value;
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Default comparison operator renderer.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Handles EQ/NE/GT/GTE/LT/LTE/LIKE/ILIKE predicate rendering.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultBetweenAstOperatorHandler.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/operator/provider/DefaultBetweenAstOperatorHandler.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DefaultBetweenAstOperatorHandler.java
// Purpose: BETWEEN operator renderer.
// Flow 1: Renders lower/upper bound predicate and params.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.provider;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstOperator;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core.AstOperatorHandler;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core.OperatorHandlerContext;
import org.jooq.Condition;
import org.jooq.Field;
import org.jooq.impl.DSL;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.List;

@Component
@Order()
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DefaultBetweenAstOperatorHandler implements AstOperatorHandler {
    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public boolean supports(AstOperator operator) {
        return operator == AstOperator.BETWEEN;
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public Condition buildCondition(Field<Object> field, Object value, AstOperator operator, OperatorHandlerContext context) {
        if (!(value instanceof List<?> list) || list.size() < 2) {
            return DSL.trueCondition();
        }
        return DSL.condition("{0} BETWEEN {1} AND {2}", field, context.nextParam(list.get(0)), context.nextParam(list.get(1)));
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String buildSql(Field<Object> field, Object value, AstOperator operator, OperatorHandlerContext context) {
        if (!(value instanceof List<?> list) || list.size() < 2) {
            return "";
        }
        String p1 = context.nextParamKey(list.get(0));
        String p2 = context.nextParamKey(list.get(1));
        return field + " BETWEEN :" + p1 + " AND :" + p2;
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String sqlToken(AstOperator operator) {
        return "BETWEEN";
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Default BETWEEN operator renderer.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Renders BETWEEN with lower/upper bound validation and bindings.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

#### `DefaultInAstOperatorHandler.java`

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultInAstOperatorHandler.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/operator/provider/DefaultInAstOperatorHandler.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DefaultInAstOperatorHandler.java
// Purpose: IN/NOT_IN operator renderer.
// Flow 1: Expands list values into deterministic named parameters.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.provider;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstOperator;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core.AstOperatorHandler;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core.OperatorHandlerContext;
import org.jooq.Condition;
import org.jooq.Field;
import org.jooq.Param;
import org.jooq.impl.DSL;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

@Component
@Order()
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DefaultInAstOperatorHandler implements AstOperatorHandler {
    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public boolean supports(AstOperator operator) {
        return operator == AstOperator.IN || operator == AstOperator.NOT_IN;
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public Condition buildCondition(Field<Object> field, Object value, AstOperator operator, OperatorHandlerContext context) {
        if (!(value instanceof List<?> list) || list.isEmpty()) {
            return DSL.trueCondition();
        }
        List<Field<?>> params = new ArrayList<>();
        for (Object item : list) {
            Param<Object> p = context.nextParam(item);
            params.add(p);
        }
        return operator == AstOperator.NOT_IN ? field.notIn(params) : field.in(params);
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String buildSql(Field<Object> field, Object value, AstOperator operator, OperatorHandlerContext context) {
        if (!(value instanceof List<?> list) || list.isEmpty()) {
            return "";
        }
        List<String> placeholders = new ArrayList<>();
        for (Object item : list) {
            placeholders.add(":" + context.nextParamKey(item));
        }
        String keyword = operator == AstOperator.NOT_IN ? "NOT IN" : "IN";
        return field + " " + keyword + " (" + String.join(", ", placeholders) + ")";
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String sqlToken(AstOperator operator) {
        return operator == AstOperator.NOT_IN ? "NOT IN" : "IN";
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Default IN/NOT_IN operator renderer.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Renders IN lists with deterministic named parameter expansion.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultNullCheckAstOperatorHandler.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/operator/provider/DefaultNullCheckAstOperatorHandler.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DefaultNullCheckAstOperatorHandler.java
// Purpose: IS_NULL/IS_NOT_NULL operator renderer.
// Flow 1: Renders null checks without value binding.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.provider;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstOperator;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core.AstOperatorHandler;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.operator.core.OperatorHandlerContext;
import org.jooq.Condition;
import org.jooq.Field;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
@Order()
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DefaultNullCheckAstOperatorHandler implements AstOperatorHandler {
    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public boolean supports(AstOperator operator) {
        return operator == AstOperator.IS_NULL || operator == AstOperator.IS_NOT_NULL;
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public Condition buildCondition(Field<Object> field, Object value, AstOperator operator, OperatorHandlerContext context) {
        return operator == AstOperator.IS_NULL ? field.isNull() : field.isNotNull();
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String buildSql(Field<Object> field, Object value, AstOperator operator, OperatorHandlerContext context) {
        return field + " " + sqlToken(operator);
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String sqlToken(AstOperator operator) {
        return operator == AstOperator.IS_NULL ? "IS NULL" : "IS NOT NULL";
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Default IS_NULL/IS_NOT_NULL operator renderer.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Renders null-check predicates without value bindings.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

#### `AstWindowFunctionHandler.java`

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstWindowFunctionHandler.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/window/core/AstWindowFunctionHandler.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// AstWindowFunctionHandler.java
// Purpose: Window function renderer contract.
// Flow 1: Renders supported window function expressions.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.window.core;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalWindowSpec;

// Primary type declaration for this component.
public interface AstWindowFunctionHandler {
    boolean supports(String functionName);

    String renderExpression(String overClause, CanonicalWindowSpec windowSpec);
}

`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Window function rendering contract.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Compiles specific window function nodes to SQL expressions.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstWindowFunctionHandlerRegistry.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/handler/window/core/AstWindowFunctionHandlerRegistry.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// AstWindowFunctionHandlerRegistry.java
// Purpose: Window function renderer registry.
// Flow 1: Selects handler by AST window.function key.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.window.core;

import org.springframework.core.annotation.AnnotationAwareOrderComparator;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

@Component
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class AstWindowFunctionHandlerRegistry {
    private final List<AstWindowFunctionHandler> handlers;

    public AstWindowFunctionHandlerRegistry(List<AstWindowFunctionHandler> handlers) {
        List<AstWindowFunctionHandler> sorted = new ArrayList<>(handlers == null ? List.of() : handlers);
        AnnotationAwareOrderComparator.sort(sorted);
        this.handlers = List.copyOf(sorted);
    }

// Resolves runtime strategy/handler/value using current semantic context.
    public AstWindowFunctionHandler resolve(String functionName) {
        if (functionName == null || functionName.isBlank()) {
            return null;
        }
        for (AstWindowFunctionHandler handler : handlers) {
            if (handler.supports(functionName)) {
                return handler;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }
}

`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Window function registry.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Resolves function renderer by window.function value.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

{`// DefaultRowNumberWindowFunctionHandler.java
// Purpose: ROW_NUMBER window renderer.
// Flow 1: Builds ROW_NUMBER() OVER(...) projection fragment.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.window.provider;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalWindowSpec;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.core.SemanticSqlConstants;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.handler.window.core.AstWindowFunctionHandler;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
@Order()
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DefaultRowNumberWindowFunctionHandler implements AstWindowFunctionHandler {
    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public boolean supports(String functionName) {
        return functionName != null && SemanticSqlConstants.WINDOW_FN_ROW_NUMBER.equalsIgnoreCase(functionName);
    }

    @Override
// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public String renderExpression(String overClause, CanonicalWindowSpec windowSpec) {
        if (overClause == null || overClause.isBlank()) {
            return "ROW_NUMBER() OVER ()";
        }
        return "ROW_NUMBER() OVER (" + overClause + ")";
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

- Runtime role: ROW_NUMBER window renderer.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Builds ROW_NUMBER() OVER(partition/order) SQL fragment.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSemanticSqlPolicyValidator.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/sql/policy/DefaultSemanticSqlPolicyValidator.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DefaultSemanticSqlPolicyValidator.java
// Purpose: Default SQL policy validator.
// Flow 1: Enforces SELECT-only and policy constraints pre-execution.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.policy;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.sql.core.*;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.McpSqlGuardrail;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.stage.context.SemanticQueryContext;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
@Order()
@RequiredArgsConstructor
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DefaultSemanticSqlPolicyValidator implements SemanticSqlPolicyValidator {

    private final McpSqlGuardrail sqlGuardrail;

    @Override
// Validates contract/safety rules before downstream execution.
    public void validate(CompiledSql compiledSql, SemanticQueryContext context) {
        if (compiledSql == null || compiledSql.sql() == null || compiledSql.sql().isBlank()) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Compiled SQL is empty for semantic query.");
        }
        sqlGuardrail.assertReadOnly(compiledSql.sql(), "semantic.query");
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Default policy validator implementation.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Enforces guardrails and raises deterministic policy errors before SQL execution.
  - 2) Participates in deterministic SQL compile pipeline before execute stage uses CompiledSql.

<CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticResultSummarizer.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/summary/SemanticResultSummarizer.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// SemanticResultSummarizer.java
// Purpose: Summary renderer contract.
// Flow 1: Defines summary API used by result-summary stage.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.summary;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.execute.SemanticExecutionResult;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.stage.context.SemanticQueryContext;

// Primary type declaration for this component.
public interface SemanticResultSummarizer {

    default boolean supports(SemanticQueryContext context) {
        return true;
    }

    String summarize(SemanticExecutionResult result, SemanticQueryContext context);

#### `DefaultSemanticResultSummarizer.java`

<div className="ce-ast-backlink-wrap">
  <a className="ce-ast-backlink" href="#result-summary-wrapper-order" title="Back to result summary/wrapper execution order" aria-label="Back to result summary/wrapper execution order">
    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12 5l-5 5h3v7h4v-7h3l-5-5zM5 19h14v2H5z" fill="currentColor"/></svg>

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultSemanticResultSummarizer.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/summary/DefaultSemanticResultSummarizer.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DefaultSemanticResultSummarizer.java
// Purpose: Default semantic summary renderer.
// Flow 1: Formats execution rows into concise summary/table output.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.summary;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.execute.SemanticExecutionResult;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.stage.context.SemanticQueryContext;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;

@Component
@Order()
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class DefaultSemanticResultSummarizer implements SemanticResultSummarizer {

    @Override
// Builds user-facing summary text/table from execution payload.
    public String summarize(SemanticExecutionResult result, SemanticQueryContext context) {
        if (result == null) {
            return "No result generated.";
        }
        if (result.rowCount() == 0) {
            return "No matching records found.";
        }
        return buildMarkdownTable(result);
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private String buildMarkdownTable(SemanticExecutionResult result) {
        List<Map<String, Object>> rows = result.rows() == null ? List.of() : result.rows();
        if (rows.isEmpty()) {
            return "Found " + result.rowCount() + " matching record(s).";
        }

        List<String> headers = new ArrayList<>();
        Map<String, Object> first = rows.getFirst();
        if (first != null) {
            headers.addAll(first.keySet().stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).map(String::valueOf).toList());
        }
        if (headers.isEmpty()) {
            return "Found " + result.rowCount() + " matching record(s).";
        }

        StringBuilder out = new StringBuilder();
        out.append("Found ").append(result.rowCount()).append(" matching record(s).").append("\n\n");
        out.append("| ").append(String.join(" | ", headers)).append(" |").append("\n");
        out.append("| ");
        for (int i = 0; i < headers.size(); i++) {
            out.append("---");
            if (i < headers.size() - 1) {
                out.append(" | ");
            }
        }
        out.append(" |").append("\n");

        for (Map<String, Object> row : rows) {
            out.append("| ");
            for (int i = 0; i < headers.size(); i++) {
                String header = headers.get(i);
                Object value = row == null ? null : row.get(header);
                out.append(escapeCell(stringify(value)));
                if (i < headers.size() - 1) {
                    out.append(" | ");
                }
            }
            out.append(" |").append("\n");
        }
        return out.toString().trim();
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private String stringify(Object value) {
        if (value == null) {
            return "";
        }
        return String.valueOf(value);
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private String escapeCell(String text) {
        if (text == null || text.isBlank()) {
            return "";
        }
        return text
                .replace("|", "\\|")
                .replace("\n", "<br/>")
                .replace("\r", "");
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Default summarizer implementation for semantic query results.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Builds concise markdown/table output and fallback messages from execution rows.
  - 2) Feeds final assistant output shaping and runtime tool response consistency.

#### `SemanticQueryRuntimeService.java`

<div className="ce-ast-backlink-wrap">
  <a className="ce-ast-backlink" href="#result-summary-wrapper-order" title="Back to result summary/wrapper execution order" aria-label="Back to result summary/wrapper execution order">
    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12 5l-5 5h3v7h4v-7h3l-5-5zM5 19h14v2H5z" fill="currentColor"/></svg>

<CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticQueryRuntimeService.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/runtime/core/SemanticQueryRuntimeService.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// SemanticQueryRuntimeService.java
// Purpose: Orchestrates end-to-end semantic stage execution.
// Flow 1: Builds SemanticQueryContext and stage pipeline runtime state.
// Flow 2: Runs stage lifecycle with deterministic order and interceptors.
// Flow 3: Captures runtime errors and emits final status metadata.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.core;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.audit.AuditService;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.audit.ConvEngineAuditStage;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.config.ConvEngineMcpConfig;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticModelRegistry;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.stage.context.SemanticQueryContext;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.stage.core.SemanticQueryStage;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.pipeline.SemanticStagePipeline;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.runtime.pipeline.SemanticStagePipelineFactory;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.session.EngineSession;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.transport.verbose.VerboseMessagePublisher;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.ObjectProvider;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.AnnotationAwareOrderComparator;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.time.temporal.TemporalAccessor;

@Component
@RequiredArgsConstructor
// Primary type declaration for this component.
public class SemanticQueryRuntimeService {

    private final ConvEngineMcpConfig mcpConfig;
    private final SemanticModelRegistry modelRegistry;
    private final SemanticStagePipelineFactory stagePipelineFactory;
    private final ObjectProvider<List<SemanticQueryStageInterceptor>> stageInterceptorsProvider;
    private final AuditService auditService;
    private final VerboseMessagePublisher verbosePublisher;

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    public Map<String, Object> plan(String question, EngineSession session) {
        ConvEngineMcpConfig.Db.Semantic cfg = mcpConfig.getDb() == null ? new ConvEngineMcpConfig.Db.Semantic() : mcpConfig.getDb().getSemantic();
        if (!cfg.isEnabled()) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Semantic query mode is disabled. Enable convengine.mcp.db.semantic.enabled=true");
        }
        String mode = mcpConfig.getDb() == null || mcpConfig.getDb().getQuery() == null
                ? ""
                : String.valueOf(mcpConfig.getDb().getQuery().getMode());
        if (!"semantic".equalsIgnoreCase(mode)) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Semantic runtime invoked while convengine.mcp.db.query.mode is not 'semantic'. current=" + mode);
        }

        List<SemanticQueryStageInterceptor> stageInterceptors = stageInterceptorsProvider.getIfAvailable(List::of);
        AnnotationAwareOrderComparator.sort(stageInterceptors);

        try {
            String safeQuestion = question == null ? "" : question;
            SemanticQueryContext context = new SemanticQueryContext(safeQuestion, session);
            SemanticStagePipeline stagePipeline = stagePipelineFactory.create();
            for (SemanticQueryStage stage : stagePipeline.stages()) {
                if (stage == null || !stage.supports(context)) {
                    continue;
                }
                publishBefore(stageInterceptors, stage.stageCode(), session, context);
                try {
                    stage.execute(context);
                    publishAfter(stageInterceptors, stage.stageCode(), session, context);
                } catch (Exception stageError) {
                    publishStageError(stage, context, session, stageError);
                    throw stageError;
                }
            }

            Map<String, Object> out = new LinkedHashMap<>();
            out.put("mode", "semantic");
            out.put("question", safeQuestion);
            out.put("semanticModelVersion", modelRegistry.getModel().version());
            out.put("retrieval", context.retrieval());
            out.put("joinPath", context.joinPath());
            out.put("ast", context.astGeneration() == null ? null : context.astGeneration().ast());
            out.put("astVersion", context.astGeneration() == null ? null : context.astGeneration().astVersion());
            out.put("astRawJson", context.astGeneration() == null ? null : context.astGeneration().rawJson());
            out.put("astRepaired", context.astGeneration() != null && context.astGeneration().repaired());
            out.put("canonicalAst", context.canonicalAst());
            out.put("astValidation", context.astValidation());
            out.put("compiledSql", context.compiledSql() == null ? null : context.compiledSql().sql());
            out.put("compiledSqlParams", context.compiledSql() == null ? null : sanitizeMap(context.compiledSql().params()));
            out.put("execution", context.executionResult());
            out.put("summary", context.summary());
            out.put("_meta", buildMeta(context, "runtime", "COMPLETED"));
            out.put("next", "completed");
            return out;
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            publishRuntimeError(session, ex);
            for (SemanticQueryStageInterceptor interceptor : stageInterceptors) {
                if (interceptor != null && interceptor.supports(session)) {
                    interceptor.onError("runtime", session, ex);
                }
            }
            throw ex;
        }
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private void publishBefore(List<SemanticQueryStageInterceptor> interceptors, String stage, EngineSession session, Object payload) {
        for (SemanticQueryStageInterceptor interceptor : interceptors) {
            if (interceptor != null && interceptor.supports(session)) {
                interceptor.beforeStage(stage, session, payload);
            }
        }
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private void publishAfter(List<SemanticQueryStageInterceptor> interceptors, String stage, EngineSession session, Object payload) {
        for (SemanticQueryStageInterceptor interceptor : interceptors) {
            if (interceptor != null && interceptor.supports(session)) {
                interceptor.afterStage(stage, session, payload);
            }
        }
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private void publishRuntimeError(EngineSession session, Exception error) {
        UUID conversationId = session == null ? null : session.getConversationId();
        if (conversationId == null) {
            return;
        }
        Map<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        payload.put("component", "semantic-query");
        payload.put("errorClass", error == null ? null : error.getClass().getName());
        payload.put("errorMessage", error == null ? null : error.getMessage());
        String determinant = ConvEngineAuditStage.RUNTIME_ERROR.name();
        auditService.audit(determinant, conversationId, payload);
        if (verbosePublisher != null) {
            verbosePublisher.publish(
                    session,
                    "SemanticQueryRuntimeService",
                    determinant,
                    null,
                    resolveToolCode(),
                    true,
                    payload
            );
        }
    }

    private void publishStageError(SemanticQueryStage stage,
                                   SemanticQueryContext context,
                                   EngineSession session,
                                   Exception error) {
        UUID conversationId = session == null ? null : session.getConversationId();
        if (conversationId == null || stage == null || context == null) {
            return;
        }
        String determinant = stageErrorDeterminant(stage);
        Map<String, Object> payload = stagePayload("ERROR", stage, context, error);
        auditService.audit(determinant, conversationId, payload);
        if (verbosePublisher != null) {
            verbosePublisher.publish(
                    session,
                    stage.getClass().getSimpleName(),
                    determinant,
                    null,
                    resolveToolCode(),
                    true,
                    payload
            );
        }
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private String stageErrorDeterminant(SemanticQueryStage stage) {
        if (stage == null) {
            return "UNKNOWN_ERROR";
        }
        String stageCode = stage.stageCode() == null ? "" : stage.stageCode();
        String normalized = stageCode.trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll("[^A-Z0-9]+", "_");
        if (normalized.isBlank()) {
            normalized = "UNKNOWN";
        }
        return normalized + "_ERROR";
    }

    private Map<String, Object> stagePayload(String lifecycle,
                                             SemanticQueryStage stage,
                                             SemanticQueryContext context,
                                             Exception error) {
        Map<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        payload.put("component", "semantic-query");
        payload.put("lifecycle", lifecycle);
        payload.put("stageCode", stage.stageCode());
        payload.put("stageClass", stage.getClass().getSimpleName());
        payload.put("question", abbreviate(context.question(), 300));
        payload.put("semanticModelVersion", modelRegistry.getModel().version());

        payload.put("retrievalEntitiesCount",
                context.retrieval() == null || context.retrieval().candidateEntities() == null
                        ? 0 : context.retrieval().candidateEntities().size());
        payload.put("retrievalTablesCount",
                context.retrieval() == null || context.retrieval().candidateTables() == null
                        ? 0 : context.retrieval().candidateTables().size());
        payload.put("joinPathEdgesCount",
                context.joinPath() == null || context.joinPath().edges() == null
                        ? 0 : context.joinPath().edges().size());
        payload.put("joinPathUnresolvedCount",
                context.joinPath() == null || context.joinPath().unresolvedTables() == null
                        ? 0 : context.joinPath().unresolvedTables().size());
        payload.put("astEntity",
                context.astGeneration() == null || context.astGeneration().ast() == null
                        ? null : context.astGeneration().ast().entity());
        payload.put("astSelectCount",
                context.astGeneration() == null || context.astGeneration().ast() == null || context.astGeneration().ast().select() == null
                        ? 0 : context.astGeneration().ast().select().size());
        payload.put("astFilterCount",
                context.canonicalAst() == null || context.canonicalAst().where() == null
                        ? 0 : countFilters(context.canonicalAst().where()));
        payload.put("astVersion",
                context.astGeneration() == null ? null : context.astGeneration().astVersion());
        payload.put("astValid",
                context.astValidation() == null ? null : context.astValidation().valid());
        payload.put("astErrorCount",
                context.astValidation() == null || context.astValidation().errors() == null
                        ? 0 : context.astValidation().errors().size());
        payload.put("compiledSqlPreview",
                context.compiledSql() == null ? null : abbreviate(context.compiledSql().sql(), 220));
        payload.put("compiledSqlParamCount",
                context.compiledSql() == null || context.compiledSql().params() == null
                        ? 0 : context.compiledSql().params().size());
        payload.put("executionRowCount",
                context.executionResult() == null ? 0 : context.executionResult().rowCount());
        payload.put("summaryPreview", abbreviate(context.summary(), 220));
        payload.put("_db", buildDbMeta(context));
        payload.put("_meta", buildMeta(context, stage.stageCode(), lifecycle));

        if (error != null) {
            payload.put("errorClass", error.getClass().getName());
            payload.put("errorMessage", error.getMessage());
        }
        return payload;
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private Map<String, Object> buildMeta(SemanticQueryContext context, String stageCode, String lifecycle) {
        Map<String, Object> meta = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        meta.put("component", "semantic-query");
        meta.put("toolCode", resolveToolCode());
        meta.put("stageCode", stageCode);
        meta.put("lifecycle", lifecycle);
        meta.put("questionLength", context == null || context.question() == null ? 0 : context.question().length());
        meta.put("astPrepared", context != null && context.astGeneration() != null && context.astGeneration().ast() != null);
        meta.put("astValidated", context != null && context.astValidation() != null);
        meta.put("astValid", context != null && context.astValidation() != null && context.astValidation().valid());
        meta.put("sqlCompiled", context != null && context.compiledSql() != null && context.compiledSql().sql() != null && !context.compiledSql().sql().isBlank());
        meta.put("sqlExecuted", context != null && context.executionResult() != null);
        meta.put("summaryPrepared", context != null && context.summary() != null && !context.summary().isBlank());
        meta.put("astVersion", context == null || context.astGeneration() == null ? null : context.astGeneration().astVersion());
        return meta;
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private Map<String, Object> buildDbMeta(SemanticQueryContext context) {
        Map<String, Object> db = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        db.put("toolCode", resolveToolCode());
        db.put("sql", context != null && context.compiledSql() != null ? context.compiledSql().sql() : null);
        db.put("sqlPreview", context != null && context.compiledSql() != null ? abbreviate(context.compiledSql().sql(), 220) : null);
        db.put("params", context != null && context.compiledSql() != null && context.compiledSql().params() != null
                ? sanitizeMap(context.compiledSql().params()) : Map.of());
        db.put("paramCount", context != null && context.compiledSql() != null && context.compiledSql().params() != null
                ? context.compiledSql().params().size() : 0);
        db.put("rowCount", context != null && context.executionResult() != null ? context.executionResult().rowCount() : 0);
        return db;
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private Map<String, Object> sanitizeMap(Map<String, Object> source) {
        Map<String, Object> out = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        if (source == null) {
            return out;
        }
        for (Map.Entry<String, Object> e : source.entrySet()) {
            out.put(e.getKey(), sanitizeValue(e.getValue()));
        }
        return out;
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private Object sanitizeValue(Object value) {
        if (value == null) {
            return null;
        }
        if (value instanceof TemporalAccessor) {
            return value.toString();
        }
        if (value instanceof Map<?, ?> map) {
            Map<String, Object> nested = new LinkedHashMap<>();
            for (Map.Entry<?, ?> entry : map.entrySet()) {
                nested.put(String.valueOf(entry.getKey()), sanitizeValue(entry.getValue()));
            }
            return nested;
        }
        if (value instanceof Iterable<?> iterable) {
            List<Object> items = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
            for (Object item : iterable) {
                items.add(sanitizeValue(item));
            }
            return items;
        }
        return value;
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private int countFilters(com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalFilterGroup group) {
        if (group == null) {
            return 0;
        }
        int count = group.conditions() == null ? 0 : group.conditions().size();
        if (group.groups() != null) {
            for (var child : group.groups()) {
                count += countFilters(child);
            }
        }
        return count;
    }

// Resolves runtime strategy/handler/value using current semantic context.
    private String resolveToolCode() {
        ConvEngineMcpConfig.Db.Semantic cfg = mcpConfig.getDb() == null ? new ConvEngineMcpConfig.Db.Semantic() : mcpConfig.getDb().getSemantic();
        if (cfg == null || cfg.getToolCode() == null || cfg.getToolCode().isBlank()) {
            return "db.semantic.query";
        }
        return cfg.getToolCode().trim();
    }

// Helper method used by the main runtime flow in this component.
    private String abbreviate(String text, int max) {
        if (text == null || text.isBlank()) {
            return text;
        }
        if (max <= 0 || text.length() <= max) {
            return text;
        }
        return text.substring(0, max) + "...";
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Runtime wrapper/orchestrator around full semantic stage pipeline.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Wraps stage execution, error handling, and top-level runtime envelope returned to tool layer.
  - 2) Feeds final assistant output shaping and runtime tool response consistency.


## AST Deep Dive

This section explains the AST package folder-by-folder and how one user sentence is transformed into deterministic SQL-safe structure.

<Highlight type="info" title="What AST layer actually does">
The AST layer is the semantic contract between LLM output and SQL compiler input.
- LLM can propose shape.
- AST layer normalizes, canonicalizes, and validates that shape.
- SQL compiler never compiles raw user text.
</Highlight>

### Folder map and runtime responsibility

<DbTable
  title="AST package map"
  columns={["Folder", "Primary classes", "Responsibility"]}
  rows={[
    ["ast/core", "SemanticQueryAstV1, AstFilter, AstFilterGroup, AstSort, AstOperator", "Versioned incoming AST contract from LLM JSON."],
    ["ast/normalize", "DefaultAstNormalizer", "Field alias normalization + deterministic rule application."],
    ["ast/version", "V1CanonicalAstMapper, AstCanonicalizer", "Convert V1 payload to canonical internal model."],
    ["ast/canonical", "CanonicalAst, CanonicalFilterGroup, CanonicalSubquerySpec", "Compiler-facing strict AST model."],
    ["ast/validate", "DefaultAstValidator, AstValidationResult", "Strict semantic validation before SQL compile."]
  ]}
/>

### Step-by-step with one real conversation

User ask:
- `show billbank gaps with request and order details`

#### 1) `ast/core`: parse raw JSON into typed AST (`SemanticQueryAstV1`)

<CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticQueryAstV1 core shape" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/core/SemanticQueryAstV1.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;

import java.util.List;

public record SemanticQueryAstV1(
        @JsonProperty("astVersion") String astVersion,
        String entity,
        List<String> select,
        List<AstProjection> projections,
        List<AstFilter> filters,
        AstFilterGroup where,
        @JsonProperty("time_range") AstTimeRange timeRange,
        @JsonProperty("exists") List<AstExistsBlock> existsBlocks,
        @JsonProperty("subquery_filters") List<AstSubqueryFilter> subqueryFilters,
        @JsonProperty("group_by") List<String> groupBy,
        List<String> metrics,
        List<AstWindowSpec> windows,
        List<AstSort> sort,
        AstFilterGroup having,
        Integer limit,
        Integer offset,
        Boolean distinct,
        @JsonProperty("join_hints") List<AstJoinHint> joinHints
) {
    public SemanticQueryAstV1 {
        astVersion = astVersion == null || astVersion.isBlank() ? "v1" : astVersion.trim();
        select = select == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(select);
        projections = projections == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(projections);
        filters = filters == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(filters);
        existsBlocks = existsBlocks == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(existsBlocks);
        subqueryFilters = subqueryFilters == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(subqueryFilters);
        groupBy = groupBy == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groupBy);
        metrics = metrics == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(metrics);
        windows = windows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(windows);
        sort = sort == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sort);
        joinHints = joinHints == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(joinHints);
        distinct = distinct != null && distinct;
        offset = offset == null || offset < 0 ? 0 : offset;
    }
}`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

<CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticQueryAstV1 explained line-by-line" language="java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// version tag from LLM payload; defaulted to v1 if missing
@JsonProperty("astVersion") String astVersion

// business entity chosen for this query (Account, DisconnectRequest, etc.)
String entity

// plain projection list from LLM
List<String> select

// richer projection form (field + alias)
List<AstProjection> projections

// flat filters (legacy/parallel to where tree)
List<AstFilter> filters

// recursive boolean tree (AND/OR/NOT)
AstFilterGroup where

// optional time range macro block (time_range in JSON)
@JsonProperty("time_range") AstTimeRange timeRange

// EXISTS / NOT EXISTS blocks
@JsonProperty("exists") List<AstExistsBlock> existsBlocks

// scalar subquery comparisons
@JsonProperty("subquery_filters") List<AstSubqueryFilter> subqueryFilters

// group-by fields
@JsonProperty("group_by") List<String> groupBy

// metric keys from semantic model (e.g., billbank_gap_count)
List<String> metrics

// window function declarations (ROW_NUMBER etc.)
List<AstWindowSpec> windows

// ordering
List<AstSort> sort

// having tree for aggregate queries
AstFilterGroup having

// pagination
Integer limit
Integer offset

// DISTINCT select mode
Boolean distinct

// optional join hints
@JsonProperty("join_hints") List<AstJoinHint> joinHints

// canonical constructor behavior:
// 1) default astVersion to v1
// 2) make list fields null-safe immutable copies
// 3) normalize distinct to boolean false when null
// 4) normalize negative/null offset to 0`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What it means:
- Every top-level query intent is explicit and typed.
- This avoids dynamic map parsing later in compiler stages.

#### 2) `ast/core`: operator normalization (`AstFilter`, `AstSubqueryFilter`)

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstFilter.operatorEnum() alias normalization" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/core/AstFilter.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`String normalized = op.trim().toUpperCase().replace("-", "_").replace(' ', '_');
normalized = normalizeAggregateOperator(normalized);
if ("CONTAINS".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.ILIKE;
if ("IS_NOT".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.IS_NOT_NULL;
if ("IS".equals(normalized) || "NULL".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.IS_NULL;`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What it means:
- LLM/operator variants (`contains`, `IS NOT`, `NOT IN`) are normalized before validation.
- Aggregate-style tokens (`COUNT_GT`, `SUM_GTE`, etc.) are normalized to base operators.
- Prevents enum failures from natural-language operator tokens.

#### 3) `ast/normalize`: deterministic cleanup + intent rule application

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultAstNormalizer.normalize() high-level flow" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/normalize/DefaultAstNormalizer.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`String targetEntity = ast.entity();
SemanticIntentRule rule = resolveIntentRule(question, model);
targetEntity = applyForcedEntityIfConfigured(rule, targetEntity, model);

// normalize fields using alias map
normalizedSelect = normalizeFields(ast.select(), entity.fields());
normalizedSelect = pruneUnknownSelect(normalizedSelect, entity.fields().keySet());
normalizedProjections = pruneUnknownProjections(normalizedProjections, entity.fields().keySet());
normalizedWhere = normalizeFilterGroup(ast.where(), aliasMap, entity.fields());
normalizedWhere = applyFieldRemaps(normalizedWhere, entity.fields(), rule);

// demote mixed aggregate/detail when needed
if (shouldDemoteAggregateToDetail(...)) { ... }

// fail fast when normalization drops all intent-critical predicates/selects
assertNormalizationDidNotDropCriticalIntent(ast, normalized, targetEntity);`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What it means:
- Maps field aliases to canonical semantic field keys.
- Drops unknown fields that do not belong to chosen entity (including `select` and `projections`).
- Applies deterministic business overrides through `intent_rules`.
- Fails fast when normalization drops all predicates or selected fields, instead of compiling broad fallback SQL.

#### 4) behavior change now implemented (important)

<CodeBlockToggle title="Metric-aware rule override skip (new behavior)" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/normalize/DefaultAstNormalizer.java" defaultOpen={true}>
{`boolean metricRequestedByAst = metrics != null && !metrics.isEmpty();
boolean allowForceWithMetrics = rule != null && Boolean.TRUE.equals(rule.forceModeEvenWithMetrics());
boolean allowDetailForce = !metricRequestedByAst || allowForceWithMetrics;

if (!ast.metrics().isEmpty() && normalizedGroupBy.isEmpty() && questionMentionsAnyMetric(question, ast.metrics())) {
  // preserve aggregate intent for direct metric asks like "show billbank_gap_count"
  normalizedSelect = List.of();
  normalizedProjections = List.of();
}

if (allowDetailForce && rule != null && rule.forceSelect() != null) {
  // apply force_select for detail AST, or when rule explicitly allows metric override
}

boolean forceDetail = allowDetailForce
    && rule != null
    && "detail".equalsIgnoreCase(rule.forceMode());`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What it means:
- If AST carries `metrics`, detail-force is skipped by default.
- Per-rule override: when `force_mode_even_with_metrics: true`, `force_select` and `force_mode=detail` are still allowed.
- For explicit metric-name asks (for example `show billbank_gap_count`), normalizer now preserves metric intent by clearing accidental detail projections.
- Projection-drop guard allows metric-only ASTs (non-empty `metrics` with empty `select/projections`) so aggregate queries are not falsely rejected.
- SQL compiler also treats metric-only AST as metric-only SELECT and qualifies metric SQL table names to query aliases (`zp_*` -> `t*`) to avoid PostgreSQL FROM-clause errors.
- This keeps aggregation safe globally while enabling explicit business-intent exceptions.

#### 5) `ast/version`: V1 to canonical mapping (`V1CanonicalAstMapper`)

<CodeBlockToggle title="V1CanonicalAstMapper.from(...)" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/version/V1CanonicalAstMapper.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`return new CanonicalAst(
  ast.astVersion(),
  ast.entity(),
  toProjections(ast),
  toGroup(ast.where()),
  ast.timeRange(),
  toExists(ast.existsBlocks()),
  toSubqueryFilters(ast.subqueryFilters()),
  ast.groupBy(),
  ast.metrics(),
  toGroup(ast.having()),
  toWindows(ast.windows()),
  toSort(ast.sort()),
  ast.limit(),
  ast.offset(),
  Boolean.TRUE.equals(ast.distinct()),
  ast.joinHints()
);`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What it means:
- Compiler receives one strict shape (`CanonicalAst`) regardless of LLM formatting quirks.
- Mapping stage is where unsupported operators are rejected with explicit error.

#### 6) `ast/canonical`: compiler-safe model

<CodeBlockToggle title="CanonicalAst fields used by compiler" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/canonical/CanonicalAst.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`public record CanonicalAst(
    String astVersion,
    String entity,
    List<CanonicalProjection> projections,
    CanonicalFilterGroup where,
    AstTimeRange timeRange,
    List<CanonicalExistsBlock> existsBlocks,
    List<CanonicalSubqueryFilter> subqueryFilters,
    List<String> groupBy,
    List<String> metrics,
    CanonicalFilterGroup having,
    List<CanonicalWindowSpec> windows,
    List<CanonicalSort> sort,
    int limit,
    int offset,
    boolean distinct,
    List<AstJoinHint> joinHints
) { ... }`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What it means:
- This is the only AST consumed by SQL compile.
- Keeps compilation deterministic and isolated from prompt-level noise.

#### 7) `ast/validate`: strict semantic contract enforcement

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultAstValidator key checks" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/validate/DefaultAstValidator.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`validateEntityExists(...);
validateSelectedFields(...);
validateFilterGroup(...);
validateExistsBlocks(...);
validateSubqueryFilters(...);
validateWindows(...);
validateGroupingAndMetrics(...);`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

What it means:
- Unknown entity/field/operator/type mismatch fails early.
- Prevents invalid SQL from being generated downstream.

### How this AST becomes SQL (bridge summary)

<DbTable
  title="AST-to-SQL bridge"
  columns={["AST element", "Compiler impact", "Example"]}
  rows={[
    ["where.conditions", "Predicate handlers generate parameterized where SQL", "`requestStatus = :p1`"],
    ["exists.where + `$field` value", "Correlated field comparison (field-to-field)", "`exj1.zp_disconnect_id = t0.zp_disconnect_id`"],
    ["metrics + group_by + having", "Metric clause + having compile path", "`COUNT(...)`, `GROUP BY`, `HAVING`"],
    ["windows", "Window function renderer", "`ROW_NUMBER() OVER (...)`"],
    ["sort/limit/offset", "Order/pagination clause", "`ORDER BY ... LIMIT :__limit`"]
  ]}
/>

### Real AST example and normalized effect

<CodeBlockToggle title="Incoming AST (mixed detail + metric)" language="json" defaultOpen={false}>
{`{
  "entity": "BillingRecord",
  "select": ["billbankId","accountId","disconnectId","recordStatus","pendingBillAmount","updatedAt"],
  "metrics": ["billbank_gap_count"],
  "group_by": [],
  "having": {"op":"AND","conditions":[],"groups":[]}
}`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

<CodeBlockToggle title="Normalizer decision matrix (conceptual)" language="text" defaultOpen={false}>
{`if metrics present:
  if rule.force_mode_even_with_metrics == true:
    apply rule.force_select and rule.force_mode=detail
  else:
    skip detail-force overrides
else:
  detail force rules may apply`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

### What happens when AST is missing

If LLM fails to produce valid AST JSON:
- `AST_ERROR` / `AST_GENERATION_ERROR` is emitted.
- Runtime returns controlled semantic failure (no SQL compile/execute).
- `RUNTIME_ERROR` captures final failure envelope.

Each file below shows source and concise execution notes.
</Highlight>

#### `SemanticQueryAst.java`

<CodeBlockToggle title="SemanticQueryAst.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/core/SemanticQueryAst.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// SemanticQueryAst.java: Incoming LLM AST payload contract and enum/value normalization. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;

import java.util.List;

@Deprecated(forRemoval = false)
public record SemanticQueryAst(
        String entity,
        List<String> select,
        List<AstFilter> filters,
        @JsonProperty("time_range") AstTimeRange timeRange,
        @JsonProperty("group_by") List<String> groupBy,
        List<String> metrics,
        List<AstSort> sort,
        Integer limit
) {
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public SemanticQueryAst {
        select = select == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(select);
        filters = filters == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(filters);
        groupBy = groupBy == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groupBy);
        metrics = metrics == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(metrics);
        sort = sort == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sort);
    }

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public SemanticQueryAstV1 toV1() {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new SemanticQueryAstV1(
                "v1",
                entity,
                select,
                List.of(),
                filters,
                null,
                timeRange,
                List.of(),
                List.of(),
                groupBy,
                metrics,
                List.of(),
                sort,
                null,
                limit,
                0,
                false,
                List.of()
        );
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Incoming LLM AST payload contract and enum/value normalization.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Defines typed AST contract node parsed from LLM JSON.
  - 2) Used by normalizer/mapper before compile.

{`// SemanticQueryAstV1.java: Incoming LLM AST payload contract and enum/value normalization. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;

import java.util.List;

public record SemanticQueryAstV1(
        @JsonProperty("astVersion") String astVersion,
        String entity,
        List<String> select,
        List<AstProjection> projections,
        List<AstFilter> filters,
        AstFilterGroup where,
        @JsonProperty("time_range") AstTimeRange timeRange,
        @JsonProperty("exists") List<AstExistsBlock> existsBlocks,
        @JsonProperty("subquery_filters") List<AstSubqueryFilter> subqueryFilters,
        @JsonProperty("group_by") List<String> groupBy,
        List<String> metrics,
        List<AstWindowSpec> windows,
        List<AstSort> sort,
        AstFilterGroup having,
        Integer limit,
        Integer offset,
        Boolean distinct,
        @JsonProperty("join_hints") List<AstJoinHint> joinHints
) {
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public SemanticQueryAstV1 {
        astVersion = astVersion == null || astVersion.isBlank() ? "v1" : astVersion.trim();
        select = select == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(select);
        projections = projections == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(projections);
        filters = filters == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(filters);
        existsBlocks = existsBlocks == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(existsBlocks);
        subqueryFilters = subqueryFilters == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(subqueryFilters);
        groupBy = groupBy == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groupBy);
        metrics = metrics == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(metrics);
        windows = windows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(windows);
        sort = sort == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sort);
        joinHints = joinHints == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(joinHints);
        distinct = distinct != null && distinct;
        offset = offset == null || offset < 0 ? 0 : offset;
    }
}
`}

#### `AstFilter.java`

<div className="ce-ast-backlink-wrap">
  <a className="ce-ast-backlink" href="#high-level-code-execution-order" title="Back to High-level code execution order" aria-label="Back to High-level code execution order">
    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
      <path d="M12 5l-5 5h3v7h4v-7h3l-5-5zM5 19h14v2H5z" fill="currentColor"/>

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstFilter.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/core/AstFilter.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// AstFilter.java: Incoming LLM AST payload contract and enum/value normalization. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core;

public record AstFilter(
        String field,
        String op,
        Object value
) {
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public AstOperator operatorEnum() {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (op == null || op.isBlank()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return AstOperator.EQ;
        }
        String normalized = normalizeOperator(op);
        normalized = normalizeAggregateOperator(normalized);
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if ("CONTAINS".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.ILIKE;
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if ("IS_NOT".equals(normalized) || "NOT_NULL".equals(normalized) || "ISNOTNULL".equals(normalized)) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return AstOperator.IS_NOT_NULL;
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if ("IS".equals(normalized) || "NULL".equals(normalized) || "ISNULL".equals(normalized)) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return AstOperator.IS_NULL;
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if ("=".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.EQ;
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if ("!=".equals(normalized) || "<>".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.NE;
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if (">".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.GT;
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if (">=".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.GTE;
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if ("<".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.LT;
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if ("<=".equals(normalized)) return AstOperator.LTE;
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return AstOperator.valueOf(normalized);
    }

    private String normalizeAggregateOperator(String normalized) {
        if (normalized == null || normalized.isBlank()) {
            return normalized;
        }
        String[] candidates = {
                "IS_NOT_NULL", "IS_NULL", "NOT_IN",
                "BETWEEN", "ILIKE", "LIKE",
                "GTE", "LTE", "GT", "LT",
                "EQ", "NE", "IN"
        };
        for (String candidate : candidates) {
            if (normalized.equals(candidate) || normalized.endsWith("_" + candidate)) {
                return candidate;
            }
        }
        if (normalized.endsWith("_NOTNULL")) {
            return "IS_NOT_NULL";
        }
        if (normalized.endsWith("_NULL")) {
            return "IS_NULL";
        }
        return normalized;
    }

    private String normalizeOperator(String raw) {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return raw == null
                ? ""
                : raw.trim()
                .toUpperCase()
                .replace("-", "_")
                .replace(' ', '_');
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Incoming LLM AST payload contract and enum/value normalization.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Defines typed AST contract node parsed from LLM JSON.
  - 2) Used by normalizer/mapper before compile.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core;

import java.util.List;

public record AstFilterGroup(
        String op,
        List<AstFilter> conditions,
        List<AstFilterGroup> groups
) {
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public AstFilterGroup {
        conditions = conditions == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(conditions);
        groups = groups == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groups);
    }

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public AstLogicalOperator logicalOperator() {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (op == null || op.isBlank()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return AstLogicalOperator.AND;
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return AstLogicalOperator.valueOf(op.trim().toUpperCase());
    }
}
`}

        String field,
        String direction,
        String nulls
) {
    public AstSort(String field, String direction) {
        this(field, direction, null);
    }

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public SortDirection directionEnum() {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (direction == null || direction.isBlank()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return SortDirection.ASC;
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return SortDirection.valueOf(direction.trim().toUpperCase());
    }

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public NullsOrder nullsEnum() {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (nulls == null || nulls.isBlank()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return null;
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return NullsOrder.valueOf(nulls.trim().toUpperCase());
    }
}
