        SemanticQueryAstV1 ast,
        String rawJson,
        boolean repaired,
        String astVersion
) {
    public AstGenerationResult(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast, String rawJson, boolean repaired) {
        this(ast, rawJson, repaired, ast == null ? "v1" : ast.astVersion());
    }

    public AstGenerationResult(SemanticQueryAst ast, String rawJson, boolean repaired) {
        this(ast == null ? null : ast.toV1(), rawJson, repaired, "v1");
    }

{`// AstNormalizeInterceptor.java: Normalization contracts and deterministic repair/cleanup implementation. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.normalize;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.*;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticModel;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.session.EngineSession;

public interface AstNormalizeInterceptor {

    default boolean supports(EngineSession session) {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return true;
    }

    default void beforeNormalize(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast, SemanticModel model, String selectedEntity, EngineSession session) {
    }

    default SemanticQueryAstV1 afterNormalize(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast, EngineSession session) {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return ast;
    }

    default void onError(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast, EngineSession session, Exception ex) {
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Normalization contracts and deterministic repair/cleanup implementation.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Hook/implementation for pre-validation AST cleanup.
  - 2) Keeps AST deterministic for downstream stages.

import org.springframework.core.Ordered;

@Order()
public class DefaultAstNormalizeInterceptor implements AstNormalizeInterceptor {

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstNormalizer.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/normalize/AstNormalizer.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// AstNormalizer.java: Normalization contracts and deterministic repair/cleanup implementation. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.normalize;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.*;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticModel;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.session.EngineSession;

public interface AstNormalizer {

    default boolean supports(EngineSession session) {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return true;
    }

    SemanticQueryAstV1 normalize(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast, SemanticModel model, String selectedEntity, EngineSession session);
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Normalization contracts and deterministic repair/cleanup implementation.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Hook/implementation for pre-validation AST cleanup.
  - 2) Keeps AST deterministic for downstream stages.


#### `DefaultAstNormalizer.java`

<div className="ce-ast-backlink-wrap">
  <a className="ce-ast-backlink" href="#high-level-code-execution-order" title="Back to High-level code execution order" aria-label="Back to High-level code execution order">
    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
      <path d="M12 5l-5 5h3v7h4v-7h3l-5-5zM5 19h14v2H5z" fill="currentColor"/>
    </svg>
  </a>
</div>

<CodeBlockToggle title="DefaultAstNormalizer.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/normalize/DefaultAstNormalizer.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// DefaultAstNormalizer.java: Normalization contracts and deterministic repair/cleanup implementation. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.normalize;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.*;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticEntity;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticField;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticIntentFilter;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticIntentRule;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticModel;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.session.EngineSession;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.ObjectProvider;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.AnnotationAwareOrderComparator;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;

@Component
@Order()
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class DefaultAstNormalizer implements AstNormalizer {

    private final ObjectProvider<List<AstNormalizeInterceptor>> interceptorsProvider;

    @Override
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public SemanticQueryAstV1 normalize(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast, SemanticModel model, String selectedEntity, EngineSession session) {
        List<AstNormalizeInterceptor> interceptors = interceptorsProvider.getIfAvailable(List::of);
        AnnotationAwareOrderComparator.sort(interceptors);
        // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
        for (AstNormalizeInterceptor interceptor : interceptors) {
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (interceptor != null && interceptor.supports(session)) {
                interceptor.beforeNormalize(ast, model, selectedEntity, session);
            }
        }
        try {
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (ast == null || model == null || model.entities() == null) {
                // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
                return ast;
            }
            String question = resolveQuestion(session);
            SemanticIntentRule rule = resolveIntentRule(question, model);
            String targetEntity = (ast.entity() == null || ast.entity().isBlank()) ? selectedEntity : ast.entity();
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (rule != null && rule.forceEntity() != null && !rule.forceEntity().isBlank()
                    && model.entities().containsKey(rule.forceEntity())) {
                targetEntity = rule.forceEntity();
            }
            SemanticEntity entity = model.entities().get(targetEntity);
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (entity == null || entity.fields() == null || entity.fields().isEmpty()) {
                // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
                return ast;
            }
            Map<String, String> aliasToField = buildFieldAliasMap(entity.fields());

            List<String> normalizedSelect = ast.select().stream()
                    .map(field -> normalizeField(field, aliasToField, entity.fields()))
                    .toList();
            List<AstFilter> normalizedFilters = ast.filters().stream()
                    .map(filter -> filter == null ? null : new AstFilter(
                            normalizeField(filter.field(), aliasToField, entity.fields()),
                            filter.op(),
                            filter.value()))
                    .toList();
            List<AstSort> normalizedSort = ast.sort().stream()
                    .map(sort -> sort == null ? null : new AstSort(
                            normalizeField(sort.field(), aliasToField, entity.fields()),
                            sort.direction(),
                            sort.nulls()))
                    .toList();
            List<String> normalizedGroupBy = ast.groupBy().stream()
                    .map(field -> normalizeField(field, aliasToField, entity.fields()))
                    .toList();
            List<AstProjection> normalizedProjections = ast.projections().stream()
                    .map(projection -> projection == null ? null : new AstProjection(
                            normalizeField(projection.field(), aliasToField, entity.fields()),
                            projection.alias()))
                    .toList();
            AstFilterGroup normalizedWhere = normalizeFilterGroup(ast.where(), aliasToField, entity.fields());
            AstFilterGroup normalizedHaving = normalizeFilterGroup(ast.having(), aliasToField, entity.fields());

            Set<String> metricNames = model.metrics() == null ? Set.of() : model.metrics().keySet();
            boolean demoteToDetail = shouldDemoteAggregateToDetail(
                    normalizedSelect,
                    normalizedProjections,
                    normalizedGroupBy,
                    ast.metrics(),
                    metricNames
            );

            List<AstFilter> effectiveFilters = normalizedFilters;
            List<AstSort> effectiveSort = normalizedSort;
            List<String> effectiveGroupBy = normalizedGroupBy;
            List<String> effectiveMetrics = ast.metrics();
            AstFilterGroup effectiveWhere = normalizedWhere;
            AstFilterGroup effectiveHaving = normalizedHaving;

            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (demoteToDetail) {
                effectiveMetrics = List.of();
                effectiveGroupBy = List.of();
                effectiveSort = dropMetricSorts(normalizedSort, metricNames);
                effectiveFilters = dropMetricFilters(normalizedFilters, metricNames);
                effectiveWhere = dropMetricFilters(normalizedWhere, metricNames);
                effectiveHaving = new AstFilterGroup("AND", List.of(), List.of());
            }

            SemanticQueryAstV1 normalized = new SemanticQueryAstV1(
                    ast.astVersion(),
                    targetEntity,
                    normalizedSelect,
                    normalizedProjections,
                    effectiveFilters,
                    effectiveWhere,
                    ast.timeRange(),
                    ast.existsBlocks(),
                    ast.subqueryFilters(),
                    effectiveGroupBy,
                    effectiveMetrics,
                    ast.windows(),
                    effectiveSort,
                    effectiveHaving,
                    ast.limit(),
                    ast.offset(),
                    ast.distinct(),
                    ast.joinHints()
            );
            normalized = applyIntentRule(normalized, entity, metricNames, rule);
            // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
            for (AstNormalizeInterceptor interceptor : interceptors) {
                // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
                if (interceptor != null && interceptor.supports(session)) {
                    normalized = interceptor.afterNormalize(normalized, session);
                }
            }
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return normalized;
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
            for (AstNormalizeInterceptor interceptor : interceptors) {
                // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
                if (interceptor != null && interceptor.supports(session)) {
                    interceptor.onError(ast, session, ex);
                }
            }
            throw ex;
        }
    }

    private Map<String, String> buildFieldAliasMap(Map<String, SemanticField> fields) {
        Map<String, String> aliasToField = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
        for (Map.Entry<String, SemanticField> e : fields.entrySet()) {
            String fieldName = e.getKey();
            SemanticField field = e.getValue();
            putAlias(aliasToField, normalizeToken(fieldName), fieldName);
            putAlias(aliasToField, normalizeToken(camelToSnake(fieldName)), fieldName);
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (field != null && field.column() != null) {
                String col = field.column();
                String colName = col.contains(".") ? col.substring(col.lastIndexOf('.') + 1) : col;
                putAlias(aliasToField, normalizeToken(colName), fieldName);
                // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
                if (colName.startsWith("zp_")) {
                    putAlias(aliasToField, normalizeToken(colName.substring(3)), fieldName);
                }
            }
            // Field aliases now come from semantic-layer.yaml (fields.<name>.aliases).
            // This keeps remap behavior model-driven and avoids hardcoded framework aliases.
            if (field != null && field.aliases() != null) {
                for (String alias : field.aliases()) {
                    putAlias(aliasToField, normalizeToken(alias), fieldName);
                }
            }
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return aliasToField;
    }

    private void putAlias(Map<String, String> aliasToField, String alias, String fieldName) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (alias == null || alias.isBlank()) {
            return;
        }
        aliasToField.putIfAbsent(alias, fieldName);
    }

    private String normalizeField(String field, Map<String, String> aliasToField, Map<String, SemanticField> knownFields) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (field == null || field.isBlank()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return field;
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (knownFields.containsKey(field)) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return field;
        }
        String normalized = normalizeToken(field);
        String mapped = aliasToField.get(normalized);
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return mapped == null ? field : mapped;
    }

    private String normalizeToken(String raw) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (raw == null) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return "";
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return raw.replaceAll("[^A-Za-z0-9]", "").toLowerCase();
    }

    private String camelToSnake(String input) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (input == null || input.isBlank()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return "";
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return input
                .replaceAll("([a-z0-9])([A-Z])", "$1_$2")
                .toLowerCase();
    }

    private boolean shouldDemoteAggregateToDetail(List<String> select,
                                                  List<AstProjection> projections,
                                                  List<String> groupBy,
                                                  List<String> metrics,
                                                  Set<String> metricNames) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (metrics == null || metrics.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return false;
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (projections == null || projections.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return false;
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (groupBy == null || groupBy.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return true;
        }
        Set<String> groupSet = new LinkedHashSet<>(groupBy);
        boolean projectionOutsideGroup = projections.stream()
                .filter(p -> p != null && p.field() != null && !p.field().isBlank())
                .anyMatch(p -> !groupSet.contains(p.field()));
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (projectionOutsideGroup) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return true;
        }
        // If select carries metric names mixed with regular fields, prefer detail mode.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return select != null && select.stream().anyMatch(metricNames::contains);
    }

    private List<AstSort> dropMetricSorts(List<AstSort> sorts, Set<String> metricNames) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (sorts == null || sorts.isEmpty() || metricNames.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return sorts == null ? List.of() : sorts;
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return sorts.stream()
                .filter(s -> s == null || s.field() == null || !metricNames.contains(s.field()))
                .toList();
    }

    private List<AstFilter> dropMetricFilters(List<AstFilter> filters, Set<String> metricNames) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (filters == null || filters.isEmpty() || metricNames.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return filters == null ? List.of() : filters;
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return filters.stream()
                .filter(f -> f == null || f.field() == null || !metricNames.contains(f.field()))
                .toList();
    }

    private AstFilterGroup normalizeFilterGroup(AstFilterGroup group,
                                                Map<String, String> aliasToField,
                                                Map<String, SemanticField> knownFields) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (group == null) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return null;
        }
        List<AstFilter> conditions = group.conditions() == null ? List.of() : group.conditions().stream()
                .map(f -> f == null ? null : new AstFilter(
                        normalizeField(f.field(), aliasToField, knownFields),
                        f.op(),
                        f.value()))
                .toList();
        List<AstFilterGroup> groups = group.groups() == null ? List.of() : group.groups().stream()
                .map(g -> normalizeFilterGroup(g, aliasToField, knownFields))
                .toList();
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new AstFilterGroup(group.op(), conditions, groups);
    }

    private AstFilterGroup dropMetricFilters(AstFilterGroup group, Set<String> metricNames) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (group == null) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return null;
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (metricNames.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return group;
        }
        List<AstFilter> conditions = group.conditions() == null ? List.of() : group.conditions().stream()
                .filter(f -> f == null || f.field() == null || !metricNames.contains(f.field()))
                .toList();
        List<AstFilterGroup> groups = group.groups() == null ? List.of() : group.groups().stream()
                .map(g -> dropMetricFilters(g, metricNames))
                .toList();
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new AstFilterGroup(group.op(), conditions, groups);
    }

    private SemanticQueryAstV1 applyIntentRule(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast,
                                               SemanticEntity entity,
                                               Set<String> metricNames,
                                               SemanticIntentRule rule) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (ast == null || entity == null || entity.fields() == null || entity.fields().isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return ast;
        }
        Map<String, SemanticField> fields = entity.fields();
        List<AstFilter> filters = pruneUnknownFilters(ast.filters(), fields.keySet());
        List<AstSort> sorts = pruneUnknownSorts(ast.sort(), fields.keySet());
        List<String> groupBy = pruneUnknownGroupBy(ast.groupBy(), fields.keySet());
        AstFilterGroup where = pruneUnknownFilters(ast.where(), fields.keySet());
        AstFilterGroup having = pruneUnknownFilters(ast.having(), fields.keySet());
        List<String> metrics = ast.metrics() == null ? List.of() : ast.metrics();

        List<String> select = pruneUnknownSelect(ast.select(), fields.keySet());
        List<AstProjection> projections = pruneUnknownProjections(ast.projections(), fields.keySet());

        boolean metricRequestedByAst = metrics != null && !metrics.isEmpty();
        boolean allowForceWithMetrics = rule != null && Boolean.TRUE.equals(rule.forceModeEvenWithMetrics());
        boolean allowDetailForce = !metricRequestedByAst || allowForceWithMetrics;

        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (allowDetailForce && rule != null && rule.forceSelect() != null && !rule.forceSelect().isEmpty()) {
            List<String> forcedSelect = rule.forceSelect().stream()
                    .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                    .filter(fields::containsKey)
                    .toList();
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (!forcedSelect.isEmpty()) {
                select = forcedSelect;
                projections = forcedSelect.stream().map(f -> new AstProjection(f, null)).toList();
            }
        }

        boolean forceDetail = allowDetailForce && rule != null && "detail".equalsIgnoreCase(rule.forceMode());
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (forceDetail) {
            metrics = List.of();
            groupBy = List.of();
            having = new AstFilterGroup("AND", List.of(), List.of());
            filters = dropMetricFilters(filters, metricNames);
            sorts = dropMetricSorts(sorts, metricNames);
            where = dropMetricFilters(where, metricNames);
        }

        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (rule != null && rule.enforceWhere() != null && !rule.enforceWhere().isEmpty()) {
            List<AstFilter> injected = rule.enforceWhere().stream()
                    .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                    .filter(f -> f.field() != null && fields.containsKey(f.field()))
                    .map(f -> new AstFilter(f.field(), f.op(), f.value()))
                    .toList();
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (!injected.isEmpty()) {
                where = appendConditions(where, injected);
                filters = appendFlatFilters(filters, injected);
            }
        }

        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new SemanticQueryAstV1(
                ast.astVersion(),
                ast.entity(),
                select,
                projections,
                filters,
                where,
                ast.timeRange(),
                ast.existsBlocks(),
                ast.subqueryFilters(),
                groupBy,
                metrics,
                ast.windows(),
                sorts,
                having,
                ast.limit(),
                ast.offset(),
                ast.distinct(),
                ast.joinHints()
        );
    }

    private List<AstFilter> appendFlatFilters(List<AstFilter> base, List<AstFilter> extra) {
        List<AstFilter> out = new java.util.ArrayList<>(base == null ? List.of() : base);
        // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
        for (AstFilter filter : extra) {
            boolean exists = out.stream().anyMatch(f -> sameFilter(f, filter));
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (!exists) {
                out.add(filter);
            }
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return List.copyOf(out);
    }

    private AstFilterGroup appendConditions(AstFilterGroup group, List<AstFilter> injected) {
        AstFilterGroup base = group == null ? new AstFilterGroup("AND", List.of(), List.of()) : group;
        List<AstFilter> out = new java.util.ArrayList<>(base.conditions() == null ? List.of() : base.conditions());
        // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
        for (AstFilter filter : injected) {
            boolean exists = out.stream().anyMatch(f -> sameFilter(f, filter));
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (!exists) {
                out.add(filter);
            }
        }
        String op = base.op() == null || base.op().isBlank() ? "AND" : base.op();
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new AstFilterGroup(op, List.copyOf(out), base.groups() == null ? List.of() : base.groups());
    }

    private boolean sameFilter(AstFilter a, AstFilter b) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if (a == null || b == null) return false;
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return Objects.equals(a.field(), b.field())
                && Objects.equals(a.op(), b.op())
                && Objects.equals(a.value(), b.value());
    }

    private List<AstFilter> pruneUnknownFilters(List<AstFilter> filters, Set<String> knownFields) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (filters == null || filters.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return List.of();
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return filters.stream()
                .filter(f -> f == null || f.field() == null || knownFields.contains(f.field()))
                .toList();
    }

    private List<AstSort> pruneUnknownSorts(List<AstSort> sorts, Set<String> knownFields) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (sorts == null || sorts.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return List.of();
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return sorts.stream()
                .filter(s -> s == null || s.field() == null || knownFields.contains(s.field()))
                .toList();
    }

    private List<String> pruneUnknownGroupBy(List<String> groupBy, Set<String> knownFields) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (groupBy == null || groupBy.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return List.of();
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return groupBy.stream()
                .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                .filter(knownFields::contains)
                .toList();
    }

    private List<String> pruneUnknownSelect(List<String> select, Set<String> knownFields) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (select == null || select.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return List.of();
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return select.stream()
                .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                .filter(knownFields::contains)
                .toList();
    }

    private List<AstProjection> pruneUnknownProjections(List<AstProjection> projections, Set<String> knownFields) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (projections == null || projections.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return List.of();
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return projections.stream()
                .filter(Objects::nonNull)
                .filter(p -> p.field() != null && knownFields.contains(p.field()))
                .toList();
    }

    private AstFilterGroup pruneUnknownFilters(AstFilterGroup group, Set<String> knownFields) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (group == null) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return null;
        }
        List<AstFilter> conditions = group.conditions() == null ? List.of() : group.conditions().stream()
                .filter(f -> f == null || f.field() == null || knownFields.contains(f.field()))
                .toList();
        List<AstFilterGroup> groups = group.groups() == null ? List.of() : group.groups().stream()
                .map(g -> pruneUnknownFilters(g, knownFields))
                .toList();
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new AstFilterGroup(group.op(), conditions, groups);
    }

    private String resolveQuestion(EngineSession session) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (session == null) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return "";
        }
        String q = trimToNull(session.getResolvedUserInput());
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (q == null) {
            q = trimToNull(session.getStandaloneQuery());
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (q == null) {
            q = trimToNull(session.getUserText());
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return q == null ? "" : q;
    }

    private SemanticIntentRule resolveIntentRule(String question, SemanticModel model) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (question == null || question.isBlank() || model == null || model.intentRules() == null || model.intentRules().isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return null;
        }
        String lower = question.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
        for (SemanticIntentRule rule : model.intentRules().values()) {
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (rule == null) continue;
            boolean anyMatch = rule.matchAny() != null && !rule.matchAny().isEmpty()
                    && rule.matchAny().stream().filter(Objects::nonNull)
                    .map(s -> s.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
                    .anyMatch(lower::contains);
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (!anyMatch) continue;
            boolean mustContainOk = true;
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (rule.mustContain() != null && !rule.mustContain().isEmpty()) {
                // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
                for (String term : rule.mustContain()) {
                    // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
                    if (term == null || term.isBlank()) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
                    if (!lower.contains(term.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
                        mustContainOk = false;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
            if (mustContainOk) {
                // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
                return rule;
            }
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return null;
    }

    private String trimToNull(String value) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        if (value == null) return null;
        String t = value.trim();
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return t.isEmpty() ? null : t;
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Normalization contracts and deterministic repair/cleanup implementation.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Takes raw V1 AST and semantic model context from runtime stage.
  - 2) Normalizes field aliases and applies deterministic intent-rule rewrites.
  - 3) Prunes unknown fields across `select`, `projections`, `filters`, `sort`, `group_by`, `where`, and `having` for selected entity safety.
  - 4) Keeps metrics-safe behavior by default, but allows per-rule override via `force_mode_even_with_metrics`.
  - 5) Emits normalized AST for canonical mapping and validation.

<CodeBlockToggle title="V1AstVersionAdapter.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/version/V1AstVersionAdapter.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// V1AstVersionAdapter.java: Version adapters and mappers that convert payloads into canonical AST. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.version;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.SemanticQueryAstV1;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalAst;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
@Order()
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class V1AstVersionAdapter implements AstVersionAdapter {

    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    private final V1CanonicalAstMapper mapper;

    @Override
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public String version() {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return "v1";
    }

    @Override
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public CanonicalAst toCanonical(AstPayload payload) {
        try {
            SemanticQueryAstV1 ast = objectMapper.readValue(payload.rawJson(), SemanticQueryAstV1.class);
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return mapper.from(ast);
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to parse/convert v1 AST payload", ex);
        }
    }
}
`}

- Detailed control flow:

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstVersionAdapterRegistry.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/version/AstVersionAdapterRegistry.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// AstVersionAdapterRegistry.java: Version adapters and mappers that convert payloads into canonical AST. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.version;

import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

@Component
public class AstVersionAdapterRegistry {

    private final Map<String, AstVersionAdapter> adaptersByVersion;

    public AstVersionAdapterRegistry(List<AstVersionAdapter> adapters) {
        this.adaptersByVersion = adapters == null
                ? Map.of()
                : adapters.stream().collect(Collectors.toMap(
                a -> normalize(a.version()),
                Function.identity(),
                (a, b) -> a
        ));
    }

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public AstVersionAdapter resolve(String version) {
        String key = normalize(version);
        AstVersionAdapter adapter = adaptersByVersion.get(key);
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (adapter == null) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("No AstVersionAdapter found for astVersion=" + version);
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return adapter;
    }

    private String normalize(String version) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (version == null || version.isBlank()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return "v1";
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return version.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Version adapters and mappers that convert payloads into canonical AST.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Version dispatch and mapping from payload to canonical AST.
  - 2) Isolates AST version concerns from compiler/runtime.


#### `V1CanonicalAstMapper.java`

<CodeBlockToggle title="V1CanonicalAstMapper.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/version/V1CanonicalAstMapper.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// V1CanonicalAstMapper.java: Version adapters and mappers that convert payloads into canonical AST. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.version;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstFilter;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstFilterGroup;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstExistsBlock;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstOperator;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstProjection;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstSort;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstSubqueryFilter;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstWindowSpec;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.SemanticQueryAstV1;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalAst;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalExistsBlock;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalFilter;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalFilterGroup;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalProjection;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalSort;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalSubqueryFilter;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalSubquerySpec;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalWindowSpec;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

@Component
public class V1CanonicalAstMapper {

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public CanonicalAst from(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (ast == null) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return new CanonicalAst("v1", "", List.of(), null, null, List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), null, List.of(), List.of(), 100, 0, false, List.of());
        }
        List<CanonicalProjection> projections = toProjections(ast);
        CanonicalFilterGroup where = toWhere(ast.where(), ast.filters());
        CanonicalFilterGroup having = toGroup(ast.having());
        List<CanonicalExistsBlock> exists = toExists(ast.existsBlocks());
        List<CanonicalSubqueryFilter> subqueryFilters = toSubqueryFilters(ast.subqueryFilters());
        List<CanonicalWindowSpec> windows = toWindows(ast.windows());
        List<CanonicalSort> sort = ast.sort() == null ? List.of() : ast.sort().stream()
                .filter(s -> s != null && s.field() != null && !s.field().isBlank())
                .map(s -> new CanonicalSort(s.field(), safeDirection(s), safeNulls(s)))
                .toList();
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new CanonicalAst(
                ast.astVersion(),
                ast.entity(),
                projections,
                where,
                ast.timeRange(),
                exists,
                subqueryFilters,
                ast.groupBy(),
                ast.metrics(),
                having,
                windows,
                sort,
                ast.limit() == null ? 100 : ast.limit(),
                ast.offset() == null ? 0 : ast.offset(),
                ast.distinct() != null && ast.distinct(),
                ast.joinHints()
        );
    }

    private List<CanonicalProjection> toProjections(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast) {
        List<CanonicalProjection> out = new ArrayList<>();
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (ast.projections() != null && !ast.projections().isEmpty()) {
            // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
            for (AstProjection projection : ast.projections()) {
                // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
                if (projection == null || projection.field() == null || projection.field().isBlank()) {
                    continue;
                }
                out.add(new CanonicalProjection(projection.field(), projection.alias()));
            }
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (out.isEmpty() && ast.select() != null) {
            // Iterates through AST nodes / fields to normalize or validate consistently.
            for (String field : ast.select()) {
                // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
                if (field == null || field.isBlank()) {
                    continue;
                }
                out.add(new CanonicalProjection(field, null));
            }
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return out;
    }

    private CanonicalFilterGroup toWhere(AstFilterGroup where, List<AstFilter> flatFilters) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (where != null) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return toGroup(where);
        }
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (flatFilters == null || flatFilters.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return new CanonicalFilterGroup(null, List.of(), List.of());
        }
        List<CanonicalFilter> conds = flatFilters.stream()
                .filter(f -> f != null && f.field() != null && !f.field().isBlank())
                .map(this::toFilter)
                .toList();
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new CanonicalFilterGroup(null, conds, List.of());
    }

    private CanonicalFilterGroup toGroup(AstFilterGroup group) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (group == null) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return new CanonicalFilterGroup(null, List.of(), List.of());
        }
        List<CanonicalFilter> conditions = group.conditions() == null ? List.of() : group.conditions().stream()
                .filter(f -> f != null && f.field() != null && !f.field().isBlank())
                .map(this::toFilter)
                .toList();
        List<CanonicalFilterGroup> groups = group.groups() == null ? List.of() : group.groups().stream()
                .map(this::toGroup)
                .toList();
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new CanonicalFilterGroup(group.logicalOperator(), conditions, groups);
    }

    private CanonicalFilter toFilter(AstFilter filter) {
        AstOperator operator = parseOperator(filter == null ? null : filter.op(), filter == null ? null : filter.field());
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return new CanonicalFilter(filter.field(), operator, filter.value());
    }

    private List<CanonicalExistsBlock> toExists(List<AstExistsBlock> existsBlocks) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (existsBlocks == null || existsBlocks.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return List.of();
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return existsBlocks.stream()
                .filter(e -> e != null && e.entity() != null && !e.entity().isBlank())
                .map(e -> new CanonicalExistsBlock(
                        e.entity(),
                        toGroup(e.where()),
                        e.notExists() != null && e.notExists()
                ))
                .toList();
    }

    private List<CanonicalSubqueryFilter> toSubqueryFilters(List<AstSubqueryFilter> filters) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (filters == null || filters.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return List.of();
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return filters.stream()
                .filter(f -> f != null && f.field() != null && !f.field().isBlank() && f.subquery() != null)
                .map(f -> {
                    AstOperator operator = parseOperator(f.op(), f.field());
                    // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
                    return new CanonicalSubqueryFilter(
                            f.field(),
                            operator,
                            new CanonicalSubquerySpec(
                                    f.subquery().entity(),
                                    f.subquery().selectField(),
                                    toGroup(f.subquery().where()),
                                    f.subquery().groupBy(),
                                    toGroup(f.subquery().having()),
                                    f.subquery().limit() == null ? 1 : f.subquery().limit()
                            )
                    );
                })
                .toList();
    }

    private AstOperator parseOperator(String op, String field) {
        try {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return new AstFilter(field, op, null).operatorEnum();
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Unsupported AST operator: " + op + " for field: " + field, ex);
        }
    }

    private List<CanonicalWindowSpec> toWindows(List<AstWindowSpec> windows) {
        // Guard clause / branch to enforce deterministic behavior.
        if (windows == null || windows.isEmpty()) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return List.of();
        }
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return windows.stream()
                .filter(w -> w != null && w.function() != null && !w.function().isBlank())
                .map(w -> new CanonicalWindowSpec(
                        w.name(),
                        w.function(),
                        w.partitionBy(),
                        w.orderBy() == null ? List.of() : w.orderBy().stream()
                                .filter(s -> s != null && s.field() != null && !s.field().isBlank())
                                .map(s -> new CanonicalSort(s.field(), safeDirection(s), safeNulls(s)))
                                .toList()
                ))
                .toList();
    }

    private com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.SortDirection safeDirection(AstSort sort) {
        try {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return sort.directionEnum();
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.SortDirection.ASC;
        }
    }

    private com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.NullsOrder safeNulls(AstSort sort) {
        try {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return sort.nullsEnum();
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return null;
        }
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Version adapters and mappers that convert payloads into canonical AST.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Maps normalized V1 AST into canonical immutable AST nodes.
  - 2) Normalizes/parses operators and throws on unsupported tokens.
  - 3) Produces compiler-ready canonical AST structure.

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstCanonicalizer.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/version/AstCanonicalizer.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// AstCanonicalizer.java: Version adapters and mappers that convert payloads into canonical AST. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.version;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.SemanticQueryAstV1;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalAst;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
public class AstCanonicalizer {

    private final AstVersionAdapterRegistry registry;
    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;

    public AstCanonicalizer(AstVersionAdapterRegistry registry, ObjectMapper objectMapper) {
        this.registry = registry;
        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
    }

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public CanonicalAst fromRawJson(String astVersion, String rawJson) {
        AstVersionAdapter adapter = registry.resolve(astVersion);
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return adapter.toCanonical(new AstPayload(astVersion, rawJson));
    }

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public CanonicalAst fromV1(SemanticQueryAstV1 ast) {
        try {
            String raw = objectMapper.writeValueAsString(ast);
            // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
            return fromRawJson(ast == null ? "v1" : ast.astVersion(), raw);
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to serialize v1 AST for canonicalization", ex);
        }
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Version adapters and mappers that convert payloads into canonical AST.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Version dispatch and mapping from payload to canonical AST.
  - 2) Isolates AST version concerns from compiler/runtime.

{`// CanonicalFilterGroup.java: Canonical compiler-facing immutable AST model. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstLogicalOperator;

import java.util.List;

public record CanonicalFilterGroup(
        AstLogicalOperator op,
        List<CanonicalFilter> conditions,
        List<CanonicalFilterGroup> groups
) {
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public CanonicalFilterGroup {
        op = op == null ? AstLogicalOperator.AND : op;
        conditions = conditions == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(conditions);
        groups = groups == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groups);
    }

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public boolean isEmpty() {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return conditions.isEmpty() && groups.isEmpty();
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

- Runtime role: Canonical compiler-facing immutable AST model.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Canonical immutable AST node consumed by validator/compiler.
  - 2) Prevents dynamic map ambiguity during SQL generation.

    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.

        where = where == null ? new CanonicalFilterGroup(null, List.of(), List.of()) : where;
        groupBy = groupBy == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groupBy);
        having = having == null ? new CanonicalFilterGroup(null, List.of(), List.of()) : having;

    }

{`// CanonicalAst.java: Canonical compiler-facing immutable AST model. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstJoinHint;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.AstTimeRange;

import java.util.List;

public record CanonicalAst(
        String astVersion,
        String entity,
        List<CanonicalProjection> projections,
        CanonicalFilterGroup where,
        AstTimeRange timeRange,
        java.util.List<CanonicalExistsBlock> existsBlocks,
        java.util.List<CanonicalSubqueryFilter> subqueryFilters,
        List<String> groupBy,
        List<String> metrics,
        CanonicalFilterGroup having,
        java.util.List<CanonicalWindowSpec> windows,
        List<CanonicalSort> sort,
        int limit,
        int offset,
        boolean distinct,
        List<AstJoinHint> joinHints
) {
    // Public API point used by runtime stages or mapper/validator/compiler flow.
    public CanonicalAst {
        astVersion = astVersion == null || astVersion.isBlank() ? "v1" : astVersion;
        projections = projections == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(projections);
        existsBlocks = existsBlocks == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(existsBlocks);
        subqueryFilters = subqueryFilters == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(subqueryFilters);
        groupBy = groupBy == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(groupBy);
        metrics = metrics == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(metrics);
        windows = windows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(windows);
        sort = sort == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sort);
        joinHints = joinHints == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(joinHints);
        where = where == null ? new CanonicalFilterGroup(null, List.of(), List.of()) : where;
        having = having == null ? new CanonicalFilterGroup(null, List.of(), List.of()) : having;
        limit = limit <= 0 ? 100 : limit;
        offset = Math.max(offset, 0);
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

- Runtime role: Canonical compiler-facing immutable AST model.

  - 1) Canonical immutable AST node consumed by validator/compiler.

<CodeBlockToggle title="AstValidationInterceptor.java source" language="java" filePath="src/main/java/com/github/salilvnair/convengine/engine/mcp/query/semantic/ast/validate/AstValidationInterceptor.java" defaultOpen={false}>
{`// AstValidationInterceptor.java: Validation contracts and strict semantic validation implementation. This file is part of semantic AST pipeline and directly influences deterministic SQL compilation safety.
package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.validate;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.*;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.graph.core.JoinPathPlan;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticModel;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.session.EngineSession;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalAst;

public interface AstValidationInterceptor {

    default boolean supports(EngineSession session) {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return true;
    }

    default void beforeValidate(CanonicalAst ast, SemanticModel model, JoinPathPlan joinPathPlan, EngineSession session) {
    }

    default AstValidationResult afterValidate(AstValidationResult result, EngineSession session) {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return result;
    }

    default void onError(CanonicalAst ast, EngineSession session, Exception ex) {
    }
}
`}
</CodeBlockToggle>

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Validation contracts and strict semantic validation implementation.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Hook/contract/result for semantic validation stage.
  - 2) Enforces fail-fast correctness before SQL compile.

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.validate;

import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Order()

package com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.validate;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.core.*;

import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.ast.canonical.CanonicalAst;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.graph.core.JoinPathPlan;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.mcp.query.semantic.model.SemanticModel;
import com.github.salilvnair.convengine.engine.session.EngineSession;

public interface AstValidator {

    default boolean supports(EngineSession session) {
        // Returns normalized/validated value for next AST stage.
        return true;
    }

    AstValidationResult validate(CanonicalAst ast, SemanticModel model, JoinPathPlan joinPathPlan, EngineSession session);
}
`}

**What this file does:**
- Runtime role: Validation contracts and strict semantic validation implementation.
- Detailed control flow:
  - 1) Hook/contract/result for semantic validation stage.
  - 2) Enforces fail-fast correctness before SQL compile.


#### `DefaultAstValidator.java`
